War Ministry Announces Adjustments of Officers: 160 Dismissals 18

(Tokyo) This morning at 10 AM, the Japanese War Ministry announced personnel changes for officers of all ranks. 160 officers are put on the waiting list (relieved of duty). The list of important officers is as follows: (1) Officers on the waiting list: Military Councilor General Hishikari Takashi, Commander of the 2nd Division Lieutenant General Hata Shunroku.

(2) Promoted to Lieutenant General: Major General Hasunuma Shigeru, Iwasa Rokuro, Murai Katsu, Matsuda Kanpei, Hiramatsu Hideo, Kawagishi Bunzaburo, Tanaka Minoru, Yamaoka Shigeatsu, Takada Tomosuke, Nagamochi Genji, Tokugawa Yoshitoshi, Kawakami Yoshihiro, Shima Shosaburo, Kasai Heijuro, and Kawamura Kyosuke, Hirooka Yoshitada.

(3) Transfers:

Commander of the Tokyo Garrison General Nishi Yoshiichi concurrently serves as Eastern Defense Commander. Commander of the North China Garrison Lieutenant General Umezu Yoshijiro is appointed Commander of the 2nd Division. Cavalry Inspector General Lieutenant General Usami Okie is appointed Commander of the 7th Division. Commander of the Infantry School Lieutenant General Sato Saburo is transferred to the General Staff Headquarters. Lieutenant General Takahashi Sadao is appointed Director of the Army Arsenal. Lieutenant General Tani Isoniko is appointed Commander of the 16th Division. Lieutenant General Kasai Heijuro is appointed Commander of the Infantry School. Lieutenant General Hasunuma Shigeru is appointed Cavalry Inspector General. Major General Tada Hayao is appointed Commander of the North China Garrison. (1st dispatch from the Chinese League)

(Tokyo) This regular reshuffle of the army has been closely watched both inside and outside the ministry prior to its announcement. The sacrifice of General Masaki and Lieutenant General Hata is said to be due to Minister of the Army Hayashi having achieved the goal of strengthening military control. Although other aspects have not attracted public attention, the allocation of talented and courageous individuals to key positions to consolidate the orthodox approach can be considered appropriate. A key figure in the new lineup is Colonel Ishiwara's appointment as Chief of the General Staff Headquarters Section. It is said that Ishiwara will now be at the core of the General Staff Headquarters and play an active role. Furthermore, the appointment of Lieutenant Colonel Muto as Chief of the Military Affairs Section of the Army Ministry, the heart of the army, and Lieutenant Colonel Kagezo as head of the Manchuria-Mongolia Section, as well as the inclusion of Lieutenant Colonel Yanagida and others, are considered excellent measures. (1st dispatch from the Domei News Agency)

(Tokyo) The Japanese War Ministry today formally announced the reshuffle order for all army officers. Regarding this reshuffle, a major upheaval had occurred beforehand, with Minister of the Army Hayashi's reshuffle proposal being strongly opposed by Inspector General of Military Education Masaki. The issue of Lieutenant General Hata being placed on the waiting list was the main point of conflict. According to the Tokyo Newspaper, this major reshuffle aims to restore internal control within the ministry that had been lost since the Manchurian Incident, to prevent factionalism within the army, and to adopt the principle of using talent appropriately in order to strengthen the army. Regarding Minister of the Army Hayashi's reshuffle, criticisms from various sectors are as follows:

(1) Criticisms from both Houses of Parliament

Since the May 15th Incident, in which young military officers assassinated Prime Minister Inukai, the upper echelons of the military have lacked control, allowing lower-ranking officers to dominate the entire army. At least, this is the impression that the world has. The public has always held the military in respect, trust, and affection, but young military officers have used secret publications and various documents to instill fear in the nation and its people, leading to a great deal of social unrest. This shift from respect, trust, and affection to fear means that this reshuffle can reduce a great deal of social anxiety. This matter has a greater impact on the political landscape and the public than the Saito and Okada cabinets. Minister of the Army Hayashi has fulfilled half of his heavy responsibilities. What deserves attention is the issue of future leadership.

(2) Criticisms from Newspapers

Regarding this reshuffle, major newspapers in Tokyo mostly praise Minister of the Army Hayashi's wise decision. The Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun, known as the mouthpiece of the military, states that the current reshuffle still has some shortcomings. The waiting list status of Generals Hishikari and Matsui is unexpected for Matsui. (The Yomiuri Shimbun also makes a similar statement, saying that Hayashi's actions towards Matsui were like "shedding tears to execute Ma Su.") Because General Matsui established the Greater Asiaism Association outside the army and engaged in various political activities, he was misunderstood by various sectors and was forced to retire due to being perceived as disrupting control. In fact, Matsui supported Minister of the Army Hayashi's control. The reason why Matsui had to retire was that Minister of the Army Hayashi considered the balance of power after Masaki's resignation and sacrificed him. The public is most concerned about Lieutenant General Hata's waiting list status in this reshuffle. There had been many rumors about Hata's actions while serving as Commander of the Kenpeitai. After General Masaki's resignation, Hata naturally could not remain in his position. It was originally planned that Lieutenant Generals Tatekawa and Koiso, and Major General Tojo of the Control Faction would advance to the central government, but they remained in their local positions. It is said that this was not Minister of the Army Hayashi's intention, and it is a regret within the ministry. It can be described as a shortcoming. As for the promotion of Colonel Ishiwara, a meritorious figure in the Manchurian Incident, to Chief of the Operations Section of the General Staff Headquarters, the appointment of Colonel Ishimoto of the Kwantung Army as head of the Investigation Unit, the transfer of Military Attaché Kagezo to head of the Manchuria-Mongolia Section of the Military Affairs Section of the Army Ministry, and the appointment of Lieutenant Colonel Hanaya as a staff officer of the Kwantung Army, all of which represent the heavy use of young military officers, are the highlights of Minister of the Army Hayashi's fourth reshuffle plan. It is said that the regular reshuffle in December will be the finishing touch to Minister of the Army Hayashi's personnel policy.

(3) Criticisms from Social Democrats

The Shikyoku Shimbun, the organ of the Social Democrats, states that this reshuffle is not a retreat of the "Western Faction" but a defeat of the "disguised hardliners." Its main point is that if General Masaki's resignation is seen as a retreat of the fascist faction, it is a mistake. The head of the disguised hardliners is in fact making the entire army even more rigid. The strongest hardliners in the army have advanced to the central government, such as Colonel Ishiwara of the Manchurian Incident being appointed Chief of the Operations Section, Lieutenant Colonel Kagezo as head of the Manchuria-Mongolia Section, and Colonel Ishimoto as head of the Investigation Unit. The future direction of the army will be determined by these middle-ranking officers. This, coupled with the reappointment of Lieutenant Colonel Hanaya as a staff officer of the Kwantung Army, makes the trend even more noteworthy. (1st dispatch from the Chinese League)

Finance Minister Takahashi Advises Japan to Exercise Restraint: Necessary Military Expenses Can Be Approved 19

Hayama – Finance Minister Takahashi, who is staying at his villa in Isshiki, Hayama, made a statement on the current situation on the 31st, saying, "The budget must be examined and determined through practical negotiations. Demands that are approved during practical negotiations and then subsequently requested again are useless. The truly necessary items should be approved from the beginning. Reinstatement requests will not be approved in principle, except for those within the scope of the troop budget that are mutually flexible between the expenses of each ministry. National defense expenses, which are absolutely necessary in light of the international situation, must be approved. However, if the army and navy compete for unnecessary expenditures in the name of national defense, then we should be humble towards the people. The war between Bolivia and Paraguay for two years caused the people to suffer terribly, which can serve as a warning. The Abyssinian problem should not lead to war. If Europe is stable, then European power will gradually reach East Asia. Therefore, Japan should exercise restraint and not make too many enemies. Regarding low interest rates, I believe that the trend of the financial world is the right one. I have no preconceived notions about this. The Bank of Japan is well aware of interest rate policies, and its judgment will be fair." (1st dispatch from the Domei News Agency)

Pacific Defense Enhancement Issue: US Navy Secretary Issues Statement: Must Be Considered After Treaty Expires: President Roosevelt Agrees With His Statement 28

(Washington) Navy Secretary Swanson stated today that after the current naval treaty expires, the issue of naval bases and fortifications on the Aleutian Islands and US islands in the Pacific Ocean must be considered. He also said that any international naval conference must discuss this issue. Swanson believes that after the Washington Naval Treaty expires at the end of 1936, the current restrictions on fortification will become invalid. Also, if the United States loses the Philippine Islands, the navy may have to be stationed elsewhere, so this issue must be considered. However, the Navy Secretary also solemnly stated that these actions will only be considered after the Washington Treaty expires. Swanson stated that the Navy Department is fully aware of Britain's shipbuilding plans, but the US shipbuilding plan will aim for the strength allowed by the treaty, at least until 1942. Regardless of the actions of other countries, the United States will not change its plans. As for the issue of replacing battleships, no decision has been made yet, but if Britain and Japan have other shipbuilding plans in 1937, the United States may also follow suit. At the same time, President Roosevelt also stated in a conversation with the press that defense issues must be considered after the naval treaty expires. Undersecretary of State Phillips said that there are no new developments in naval issues and that the State Department has not recently discussed fortification and other issues with other countries. (31st dispatch from the Kuomintang News Agency)

(Washington) Navy Secretary Swanson said, "If we lose the Philippines, we may want to advance elsewhere." But President Roosevelt stated that this is purely speculation and that all news about this is merely imaginary and fictitious. (31st dispatch from Reuters)

Los Angeles: An American government-secretly manufactured military aircraft was test-flown yesterday near the St. Vincent lighthouse on the Pacific coast. Soviet International Trade 29

(TASS Moscow dispatch, July 10) Soviet foreign trade became a surplus in 1933, and debt has been reduced to a minimum. Recently, due to increased Soviet exports and long-term credit, imports have also greatly expanded. According to the figures for the past four months of this year, Soviet exports are decreasing, while imports are increasing due to the favorable conditions of foreign orders. The decrease in exports is due to improved domestic living conditions and increased demand. However, in the past four months, Soviet foreign trade still had a surplus of 18.4 million rubles. Recently, the nature of Soviet foreign trade goods has undergone great changes. Almost all imported goods can now be manufactured domestically, so foreign imports only supplement domestic shortages and accelerate the completion of economic plans. They do not play a major role in any economic sector. For four years, machinery imports have greatly decreased, while raw materials and ordinary commodities have increased (commodities increased from 6.8% in 1931 to 15% in 1934).

Among Soviet export goods, industrial products are increasing day by day. Please see the table below:

Soviet Heavy Industry Export Goods 30

The export of machinery has increased rapidly in both absolute and relative numbers. In the first four months of last year, machinery exports were 831,000 rubles, and in the same period this year, they increased to 3.16 million rubles. Last year was the first year that the Soviet Union exported pig iron. In the first four months of last year, pig iron exports were 1,400 tons, and in the same period this year, they were 86,400 tons. Last year, Soviet pig iron exports accounted for 7% of the world's pig iron exports.

Some goods were originally imported but have become export goods due to industrial development, such as machinery, steel, cement, coal, rolled steel, electric bubbles, fertilizers, clothing, and various chemicals. From this, it can be seen that the Soviet economy is developing rapidly, and the structure of its foreign trade is also undergoing major changes.

Vietnamese Government Improves Import Tax on Chinese Goods 31

(Nanjing) After the Sino-French-Vietnamese border agreement came into effect on the 22nd of last month, the Vietnamese government fulfilled the agreement and gradually improved the treatment of overseas Chinese. Import and transit taxes on goods specified in the annex to the agreement will all enjoy the lowest tax rates currently in effect in Vietnam. The Guangdong, Guangxi, and Yunnan customs offices in our country have also received orders from the government that rice imported from Vietnam to the three provinces will all be given preferential treatment and taxed at 1.50 gold units. Coal imported into each province will be taxed at 0.89 gold units per ton. Miscellaneous grains, cement, and dried fish will be taxed at the current prevailing rates of various countries. (1st dispatch from the special correspondent)

Italy Opposes British-French Draft: League of Nations Meeting Postponed by One Day: Laval Asks Mussolini to Wait: Compromise Expected Within 24 Hours 32

(Geneva) The resolution drafted by Eden and Laval to resolve the Italian-Abyssinian dispute has been opposed by the Italian side. As a result, this afternoon's 5 PM public meeting has been postponed until tomorrow, with the time yet to be determined. At the same time, Laval has asked Mussolini not to raise objections for the time being. It is reported that the Italian government does not want the Council to be involved in Italian activities in any way. It is believed that the draft resolution submitted to the Italian and Abyssinian sides today represents the minimum requirement of the British. It is reported that the British explanation of the French original draft contains an agreement that if negotiations based on the 1906 treaty fail, the entire problem should be studied in September. The resolution lists the following five points:

(1) The League of Nations Council should interpret the scope of work of the Conciliation Committee and confirm Italy's view that the Committee is not responsible for surveying boundary lines. (2) Appoint a fifth arbitrator and ask the Conciliation Committee to follow the precedent of 1928 so that a solution can be agreed upon by September 1.

(3) The three countries that signed the 1906 treaty should immediately begin negotiations to facilitate a solution. This solution, with the cooperation of the Abyssinian government, can ensure good relations between the two countries.

(4) Both sides should conduct negotiations and submit a report on September 4.

(5) The League of Nations Council, regardless of the situation, must meet on September 4 to discuss the entire situation. It is not yet certain whether the obligation not to resort to force will be included in the resolution, but in any case, it will contain this meaning. Some quarters are quite optimistic that a compromise can be reached within 24 hours. The main obstacles to a compromise are Italy's failure to concede and announce that it will not resort to force, and Rome's opposition to the 1906 treaty. (1st dispatch from Reuters)

League of Nations Meeting the Other Day: Italy and Abyssinia Present Their Cases; Representatives of Various Countries Focus on Behind-the-Scenes Negotiations 33

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council meeting to discuss the Italo-Abyssinian issue convened at 5:00 PM today amidst a tense atmosphere. The first meeting was held in the former Disarmament Conference venue in utmost secrecy, lasting less than an hour, allowing the representatives to continue negotiations behind the scenes during the break. After the meeting, the Executive Council issued a communiqué stating that the meeting would continue tomorrow afternoon, and the countries concerned would strive to find a way to continue the arbitration and mediation work. Today's meeting began with the Abyssinian representative, Mr. Jeze, speaking first, followed by the Italian representative, Mr. Aloisi, and the British representative, Mr. Eden. All three presented preliminary information on mediation. The Chairman of the Executive Council, Mr. Litvinov, stated that the Executive Council meeting was limited to the League of Nations Covenant. The French representative, Mr. Laval, proposed adjournment. Sources with inside information claim that efforts are currently underway to find a formal solution to the Italo-Abyssinian dispute within the framework of the League of Nations, and to invoke the 1906 Tripartite Treaty to seek a basis for practical mediation. Prior to today's meeting, representatives of the countries concerned held preliminary talks. The French delegation expressed optimism, claiming that a compromise solution on procedural issues was imminent, but this optimism may be somewhat artificial. It is widely rumored here that Mr. Eden has stated that he would only agree to continue mediation if Italy guarantees not to resort to force before the League of Nations Executive Council convenes in August. (31st National Telegram)

(Geneva) Although Abyssinia is not a member of the Executive Council today, its League of Nations representative, Mr. Hawaaryat, was invited to attend, assisted by Dr. Jeze, the legal advisor to the Abyssinian delegation. First, Chairman Litvinov read the agenda and a telegram from Italian Prime Minister Mussolini regarding reservations on the scope of discussion. The Abyssinian representative then stood up to state Abyssinia's reasons and insisted that the issue of sovereignty over the seven territories should be included, and that Abyssinia reserved the right to raise all issues. Mr. Laval then proposed an adjournment to facilitate informal negotiations. Mr. Eden expressed his agreement, but stated that the Executive Council's right to expand the scope of discussion should not be restricted in any way. The attitude taken by the Abyssinian representative today was quite weak, and he did not protest the crucial point of limiting the agenda to discussing the Walwal incident, which surprised everyone. When Mr. Laval proposed adjournment, Italian representative Aloisi jumped up and said that his attendance at the meeting was only for discussing the mediation issue. After the adjournment, Mr. Litvinov, Mr. Laval, Mr. Eden, and Mr. Aloisi immediately held an informal meeting. If a consensus could be reached through private talks, the United Kingdom would accept it. However, if a consensus could not be reached, Mr. Eden would strongly request the Executive Council meeting to conduct a comprehensive discussion of the dispute. (31st Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) Messrs. Avenol, Litvinov, Laval, and Eden convened in Mr. Avenol's private office after the adjournment of the League of Nations Executive Council, seeking a satisfactory way to achieve some kind of resolution that the Executive Council must pass. It is said that Mr. Laval insisted that negotiations should be as swift as possible, as he must return to Paris on Friday or Saturday. Mr. Eden seemed less optimistic about the outcome of today's meeting. According to those close to the British delegation, the British delegation was quite dissatisfied with the lack of enthusiasm among the representatives of various countries for supporting the League of Nations. Mr. Aloisi's long conversation with Abyssinian representative Professor Jeze after the adjournment attracted general attention. (31st National Telegram)

(Beijing) An article in an Italian newspaper reveals Mussolini's hand and is detrimental to the peace efforts in Geneva. A key sentence reads, "Italy will move forward with Geneva, or without Geneva, or even in opposition to Geneva." "The solution to the Abyssinian problem must be a comprehensive solution. Opening up and assisting with force, or guaranteeing territory without accompanying military plans, will inevitably lead to a second Adowa." The article explains the security of Italian colonies, stating that only Italy can be the judge, and says, "When danger comes, we will not be assisted by anyone, and we may even be kicked when we are down. Italy does not fight under the pretext of abolishing slavery, but the abolition of slavery will naturally be the logical consequence of its policies." (1st Reuters Telegram)

Addis Ababa The King of Abyssinia has ordered the Abyssinian representatives in Geneva to strictly adhere to the instructions they have received and not to make any concessions. The King told news reporters that this instruction actually opens the way for a peaceful resolution. The Abyssinian bishops also sent a telegram to Geneva appealing for peace, saying that the attention of the world is focused on Geneva in the hope of avoiding bloodshed. (1st National Telegram)

Addis Ababa The British "Times" published a message stating that the United Kingdom, France, and other countries advocate placing Abyssinia under the trusteeship of the League of Nations and have made suggestions to the Abyssinian Emperor. Mr. Heruy, the Abyssinian Foreign Minister, has formally denied that the Abyssinian Emperor has had any contact in this regard. Those in charge further stated that this suggestion is unacceptable to Abyssinia. (31st Havas Telegram)

Addis Ababa Abyssinia is prepared to fight to the end. The whole country is filled with the spirit of war, and people of all levels are rushing to practice military skills. The formal troops are prepared to fight back vigorously when the Italian army attacks. Officials are paying close attention to the attitude of the United Kingdom in Geneva. The government is most concerned about the inability to import arms. Therefore, it is widely rumored that Abyssinia will sign a commercial treaty with Sweden on August 7, thereby canceling the Swedish arms embargo. A spokesperson for the Abyssinian government stated that Abyssinia is willing to make economic concessions to achieve mutual benefit, but if political concessions are desired, they must first come through war. (31st National Telegram)

(London) Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare recently stated in the House of Commons that there are a total of 163 British missionaries, expatriates, and their families residing within the borders of Abyssinia. The government is discussing with the British Minister to Abyssinia and the French government to seek proper solutions to protect the safety of these expatriates. Overseas Trade Minister Mr. Colville stated that the government has not prohibited the export of raw materials used for manufacturing munitions to Abyssinia. (31st Havas Telegram)

Danzig Danzig has now become a free port. Declaration of the New Dutch Government: Determined to Maintain the Gold Standard; Business Circles Greatly Relieved 35

The Hague Prime Minister Dr. Colijn stated to the press today that the Dutch government is determined to maintain the gold standard. He also said that an international conference on commerce and monetary stability should be convened as soon as possible. (31st Reuters Telegram)

The Hague After the news of the formation of Mr. Colijn's new cabinet spread, business circles were greatly relieved. Business circles had been feeling uneasy about the large outflow of gold and hoped that the establishment of a responsible government would eliminate this crisis. Mr. Colijn's choice of new cabinet members, all of whom were veterans, has drawn various criticisms from opposition newspapers. Socialist newspapers claim that the cabinet has not changed and that the previous dangerous policies will continue. The Catholic Party is taking an extremely reserved attitude, saying that the new government should be judged by its actions. Political circles predict that Mr. Colijn does not want to submit the list of new cabinet members to the parliament immediately but will suspend the parliament and submit a report when the parliament reconvenes, explaining the government's measures. At the same time, he will issue emergency orders to reorganize national affairs. The Dutch currency has gradually become stable. (31st National Telegram)

(Paris) Mr. Colijn, the newly appointed Prime Minister of the Netherlands, recently stated to the correspondent of the Paris Economic and Financial News Agency stationed in the Dutch capital, "The Dutch political unrest was quickly resolved in a matter of days, so that the guilder was not forced to devalue. Under unstable political conditions, the devaluation of the guilder would be enough to shake the economic life of the country. The activities of speculators attacking the guilder have completely failed. The government is determined to continue its past policies on monetary issues. As for restoring normal international trade relations and stabilizing international currency prices, both are urgent tasks at hand and must be completed in a short period of time. All countries should jointly negotiate to seek solutions to these two issues. If there are any serious efforts on the part of the international community regarding these issues, such as convening an international conference on currency stability, the Dutch government will naturally cooperate and will not delay." (1st Havas Telegram)

Austrian Restoration Issue: Deputy Prime Minister Forbids Military Involvement in Politics 36

(Vienna) Prince Starhemberg, leader of the Home Guard and Deputy Prime Minister, recently issued an order to the cadres of the Home Guard in Tyrol, strictly prohibiting the Home Guard from engaging in all political activities. He stated, "All soldiers should abide by the precept of non-interference in politics. For example, regarding the issue of the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty, the Patriotic League must not be divided by this issue. In the future, all informal armed groups that cannot abandon political activities will be dissolved by the government. The government is now strong and does not fear such armed groups." Starhemberg continued, "Austria's diplomatic position is not yet consolidated. Soon, Austria's independence will be guaranteed by all countries and will not be disputed. In the future, if foreign governments attempt to interfere in Austria's internal affairs, all countries that signed the Danube Pact will rise up to attack them." (31st Havas Telegram)

(Vienna) Today, a semi-official newspaper reported that the recent order by the Governor of Upper Austria prohibiting municipalities from granting honorary citizenship to members of the Habsburg dynasty will not be extended to other provinces. At the same time, local authorities throughout Austria have granted honorary citizenship to Archduke Otto in 800 cities and towns. This matter has now aroused great anger among domestic republicans and opponents of restoration. (1st National Telegram)

The United States Is Caught in a Dilemma Regarding the German Issue: Reply to the New York Incident to Be Sent on Sunday 37

(Washington) It is now apparent here that Germany's protest regarding the New York incident has placed President Roosevelt's government in a dilemma. If it apologizes to Germany, there are four difficulties: (1) The voting power of American Jews and Catholics is very large; (2) There is a strong and active minority in Congress that wants to sever diplomatic relations with Germany and will seize the opportunity to make demands if an apology is made; (3) The government itself is somewhat displeased with the Hitler government, partly because of Hitler's religious and racial policies, and partly because Germany has violated treaties and discriminated against American products and American holders of German bonds; (4) The Bremen postal ship brought this on itself because the police were in a difficult position. The government first and foremost wants to abide by all treaties and protect the flags of other countries. Secondly, it dislikes the Communist Party and does not want to condone its actions. At the same time, the New York Police Department has prepared a detailed report for the State Department's reference. The State Department's reply to Germany will probably be sent on Sunday. (31st National Telegram)

The Chahar Provincial Government Sent Personnel to Escort Mueller to Beiping: Mueller Reports on His Kidnapping and Escape; Chahar Authorities Are Negotiating to Rescue Jones 38

(Beiping) Mr. Mueller, the German journalist who was kidnapped by bandits in Guanaamagou, 50 miles northeast of Baochang in eastern Chahar, has escaped and was escorted to Beiping this morning by Mr. Zhai Weiqi, dispatched by the Chahar Provincial Government. The German Embassy, after receiving notification from Mr. Qin Dechun's residence in advance, sent personnel along with Mr. Mueller's family to the station to welcome him. After getting off the train, Mr. Mueller went directly to his private residence to rest. He is scheduled to go to the German Embassy at noon to report on his experiences of the kidnapping and escape, and to meet with Chinese and foreign reporters in the afternoon to explain the details. According to a staff member of the German Embassy, ​​Mr. Mueller and British journalist Jones left Duolun on the 27th and encountered bandits in Guanaamagou, 50 miles northeast of Baochang, at 11:00 AM on the 28th. There were more than 1,000 bandits who rushed out of the sorghum fields on both sides with complete weapons. If the Deutsch-Hua Automobile Company's vehicle they were traveling in had not been hit in the water tank, it might have escaped danger. After Mr. Mueller, Mr. Jones, etc. were kidnapped, the bandits released the driver and Mr. Liang, Mr. Mueller's servant, ordering them to report to the Baochang County Government and prepare 100,000 silver dollars, pistols, 20 machine guns, and 40 rifles, each with 20,000 rounds of ammunition, to redeem them. After Mr. Liang, etc. reported to Baochang, they went to Zhangjiakou to report to the British and German embassies separately. After Mr. Mueller was kidnapped, he was released due to language issues. British journalist Jones is still in the bandit den. It is not yet known whether Jones will be able to escape safely in the next few days. Mr. Mueller is grateful for the concern and efforts to rescue him from the Chinese government and Chinese and foreign friends after experiencing this extraordinary incident. According to semi-official sources, the Chahar Provincial Government ordered Squad Leader Zhang of the Baochang Security Team to negotiate with the bandits to rescue Jones. The process is going well, and a satisfactory result may be obtained in the next day or two. Mr. Shah and Mr. Wei, the two military attaches sent by the British Embassy, ​​are still in Zhangjiakou, assisting in everything. Mr. Xiao Zhenying will not return to Beiping for the time being due to the incident. (1st Special Telegram)

The German journalist Mueller Arrived in Beiping Yesterday

(Beiping) Mr. Mueller stated that this dangerous situation was caused by a prior agreement with the bandits that he would be temporarily released, leaving Jones in the bandit den as a hostage. After he went out, he could work with all parties concerned to redeem Jones. He also agreed with the bandits that he would fulfill their demands within the specified time to rescue Jones from danger. Otherwise, he would have to return to the bandit den and stay with Jones to the end. Therefore, if Jones can return safely within the specified time, there will be no problem. Otherwise, in order to fulfill his previous words and uphold his personal integrity and friendship, he will still leave Beiping, follow the original route to Baochang, and return to the bandit den. (1st Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Dr. Mueller, the German journalist who was kidnapped and then released, stated today that he deeply believes that Mr. Jones, a journalist from the Manchester Guardian, can also be released within 44-48 hours. Dr. Mueller arrived here in Zhangjiakou this morning to assist in the rescue of Jones. It is said that Jones's life is not in danger. Mueller also recounted the kidnapping to a Reuters reporter, saying that on Saturday, while traveling from Zhangjiakou to Duolun, soldiers resembling security guards suddenly opened fire on their car. Fortunately, everyone in the car was unharmed. The car was hit by two bullets. After he and Jones were kidnapped, they were placed in separate rooms. The bandits offered him tea, but threatened to hang Jones by tying one end of a rope to a beam and wrapping it around Jones's neck. This was just a threat and was not carried out. Soon after, they were placed in the same room. All their belongings were taken away. The bandit leader demanded a ransom of 100,000 silver dollars, 40 rifles, 20 pistols, and 60,000 rounds of ammunition. Mr. Jun, the Russian driver, and Mr. Hua, his servant, who were kidnapped with Mueller, were released immediately and sent north. The bandits treated them well, providing them with food and cigarettes. The next day at dusk, they took a circuitous route into the mountains. They saw two Chinese, one in a police uniform and one claiming to be a security team officer, riding horses. They spoke to the bandits. The person claiming to be an officer shouted to them, "We are here to rescue you!" Mueller also said, "I don't know if this statement is true, but the next day I was sent away, accompanied by the person claiming to be a security team officer and three bandits in police uniforms. The bandits instructed me to pay the ransom at the British and German embassies in Beiping. If it is not paid within ten days, Jones will be killed." At the same time, the bandits reduced the ransom to 50,000 silver dollars. Before leaving, Jones asked him to find a way to rescue him. Although Jones is young and is his first time in China, he was not alarmed or disoriented. When he arrived not far from Baochang, the bandits accompanying him asked him to ride his horse on his own. When he arrived in Baochang, the person claiming to be the security team officer was actually waiting on the road. Later, he learned that the person's name was Zhang Zhongzhi (transliteration), who seemed to have a lot of influence with the bandit leader. After Mueller arrived in Zhangjiakou, he reported the situation to Xiao Zhenying, who immediately telephoned Zhang Zhongzhi, asking him to contact the bandits and persuade them to release Jones. Xiao promised to compensate Mueller and Jones for their losses. After Mueller arrived in Beiping, he reported everything to the British and German embassies. He will go to Zhangjiakou tomorrow and, if necessary, to Baochang to assist in the rescue. Mueller firmly believes that although the bandits threatened to kill Jones if the ransom is not paid, they will definitely not harm him. Jones will be out of danger soon, or may be released within 48 hours. (1st Reuters Telegram)

Kailuan Coal Stockpiles Reduce Working Hours 41

(Tianjin) Starting from the 1st, the Kailuan Mining Bureau will reduce working hours by one day per week for each mine to avoid excessive stockpiling of coal. It has been decided that Linxi and Tangshan mines will be closed on Sundays, Zhaogezhuang will be closed on Wednesdays, Majiagou will be closed on Mondays, and Tangjiadian will be closed on Fridays. The Mining Bureau announced that workers will continue to receive bonuses during the shutdown period. This is a last resort measure because the current coal stockpiles in various places have reached more than 1.3 million tons. In Qinhuangdao alone, the coal stockpile has reached 700,000 tons. The Mining Bureau has returned 200 coal transportation vehicles to the Beining Railway since last week due to the depression in business. The total amount of coal stockpiles in each mine is also considerable. (1st Special Telegram)

(Tianjin) A message from Tangshan stated that after the collapse of the second pit of the Kailuan Zhaogezhuang coal mine, the three roadways underground were completely destroyed and there is no hope of restoration for the time being. Moldy Cigarette Tax Refund Standard Changed 50

(Nanjing) Cigarette companies in Shanghai pay unified tax immediately upon the cigarettes leaving the factory. If the cigarettes are returned due to mold, a certain percentage of the originally paid tax is refunded according to regulations. Now, the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Association has sent a letter to the Tax Affairs Department requesting a relaxation of the tax refund policy. This has been approved by the Ministry of Finance. Starting this month, the standard for moldy cigarette tax refunds will be increased from ten per thousand to twelve per thousand. However, in Guangdong, the tax refund will still be fifteen per thousand. (1st Dispatch)

Various Customs Along the Yangtze River Abolish Management of Domestic Postal Packages 54

(Nanjing) With the approval of the Inspector General of Customs and the Ministry of Finance, all procedures for managing domestic postal packages at the customs in Yichang, Shaping, Changsha, Yuezhou, Hankou, Jiujiang, Wuhu, Zhenjiang, and other places will be abolished from the 1st. In the future, the crackdown on the transportation of prohibited items and other matters will be the responsibility of the post office. At the same time, six articles of measures for the management of domestic postal packages by coastal and border customs were formulated and announced on the 1st, ordering the customs to comply. After the implementation of the new measures, the customs will be able to reduce personnel managing postal packages, and the transportation of postal packages by the post office will be more convenient. Sichuan Provincial Government Instructs Counties to Prepare Budget Standards, Emphasizing Love for the People, Frugality, and Avoiding Waste, to Put County Finances on the Right Track 80

Chengdu Communication: The Sichuan Provincial Government's move to Chengdu has been largely arranged. The central task at present is political reform. If we want to achieve political reform, personnel management and financial management are the two most urgent tasks. In terms of personnel, the provincial government has decided to expand the powers of the Civil Service Qualification Review Committee. The appointment of administrative personnel at all levels must first be reviewed and decided by the committee to prevent the appointment of unqualified people. Financial management is the responsibility of the Financial Reorganization Committee. The first step is to determine provincial and county expenditures and prepare budgets to eliminate waste. The provincial budget has been prepared by the Department of Finance and submitted to the Military Headquarters for review. The standards for county budget preparation and transitional measures were drafted at a joint meeting of the Provincial Government Financial Reorganization Committee on July 26. The provincial government has made precise revisions, focusing on considering the people's resources and striving for austerity. Yesterday, it issued a circular to all commissioners, instructing the county magistrates under their jurisdiction to strictly comply. The original order, budget preparation standards, and transitional measures are listed below.

Provincial Government Circular: "According to the ancient practice, all grains were included to determine national expenditure. This is the legacy of the budget and the constant principle of establishing a country. The county government's duty is to shepherd the people, so it should understand the people's resources and make arrangements accordingly. In the past, the counties had no governance, and expenditure was chaotic and could not be assessed. All industries were withered. This is the crux of the problem. At this time, when everything is being renewed, financial management is especially urgent. Living within our means is an iron rule that must be followed at present. However, since this is the beginning, there are no precedents to follow. It is difficult to cut off the water to quench the thirst in transitional finance. This government has solemnly discussed with the Financial Reorganization Committee and has separately discussed and decided on the budget standards for the counties this year and the hesitant period measures. These measures are issued so that county finance can be put on the right track on the one hand, and adapt to the facts on the other hand to avoid obstacles in implementation. It must be known that the people are poor and their resources are exhausted, which has reached its extreme. Saving one cent of public funds for the government is reducing one cent of suffering for the people. The salaries and income of the county magistrates are all the lifeblood of the people. You should search your conscience and not be willing to indulge in waste. The county government expenditure budget proposed by the Civil Affairs Department, although it has been submitted for review, has not yet been finalized. You should still consider the people's resources and tighten up the budget. You do not have to allocate and spend all of the estimates. Even during the hesitant period, you should avoid redundancy. You must ask the commissioner and county magistrate to consider the difficulties of the times, love the people, and be frugal. Within three days of receiving this order, you should prepare a budget and submit it to the District Commissioner's Office for review and transfer to this government for compilation before September 15. This matter concerns financial legislation and is the foundation for promoting all administration. You must strictly comply and do not treat it as a mere formality. If you delay, you will be severely reprimanded. This order."

Standard Measures: Instructions on Budget Preparation Standards and Transitional Measures for Each County. (1) The hesitant period for each county to prepare a budget and for the Special Office and Provincial Government to review the budget is limited to three months, from August 1 to October 31. (2) During the hesitant period, for local administrative affairs that have special funds, such as county administrative subsidies, judicial expenses, educational expenses, and construction expenses, the county magistrate should supervise the finance committee to temporarily audit and disburse expenses in accordance with the county government expenditure budget proposed by the Department of Civil Affairs (which has been reported for review but has not yet been finalized), ensuring that there is a surplus. The remaining funds will be used for emerging businesses. (3) During the hesitant period, for local administrative affairs that do not have special funds, such as public security expenses, finance committee expenses, the joint security office expenses, and Baojia expenses, the county magistrate should supervise the finance committee to investigate the regulations stipulated by the Military Headquarters and the provincial government, and consider the local financial situation to the extent that they can afford it. The required funds should be allocated from the remaining funds in the previous paragraph. (4) This year's budget should be prepared in accordance with the above two methods. The outline of the preparation should follow the regulations of the Military Headquarters for reorganizing local finances in bandit suppression areas, and refer to local conditions. (5) During the hesitant period, all previous surcharges should be temporarily allowed to continue to be levied for expenditure. (6) All funds collected in the lower quarter of this year during the hesitant period should be levied at half the rate. In addition to the expenditure for July, August, September and October, the remaining funds should be included in the budget income as legitimate expenditure. (7) Improper income and expenditure and wasteful expenditure should be abolished. (8) All funds collected this year should be kept by the Finance Committee. Except for legitimate expenditure from July onwards, they must not be misappropriated for other purposes or to repay old debts. (9) The old debts of Gu County should be thoroughly investigated and dealt with in a separate case. (10) Educational expenses should be based on legitimate income. If they come from taxes and there are no other funds to be allocated, they should continue to be levied as before. However, all exorbitant taxes must not be used in the name of educational expenses in the hope of preserving them. (11) The expenses of the Joint Security Office and the Baojia expenses may be budgeted at the lowest amount, limited to pens, ink, paper, and necessary office expenses. (12) If the finance committees of each county have not been established, they must be established within five days of receiving this document. (13) All illegal income from villages and districts below the county level should be stopped. (14) After the budget proposals of each county are prepared, they should be submitted to the Special Commissioner's Office for review and transfer to the Provincial Government before September 15. (15) The total amount of budgeted expenditure for this year must not exceed the previous year.

Serious Flooding in Northern Jiangsu; Yellow Water Reaches North of Pei; Copper Border Still Building Embankments 81

Xuzhou Communication: The breach of the Yellow River in Western Shandong and the influx of yellow water has caused Weishan Lake to rise three times. It is now gradually showing a tendency to become serious. Because the people of Western Shandong believed that the overflow of the Shandong water had nowhere to go and that the reeds in Nanyang Lake were blocking the flow, they cut them all down, resulting in a smooth flow of water and an unobstructed discharge. In addition, because large embankments were built in Northern Jiangsu, in addition to the Shandong Provincial Government's telegram to the Central Government, the people of Western Shandong entrusted Sun Zerang, a branch director of the Shandong Rural Construction Research Institute, to come to Xuzhou with two representatives of the people to inspect Pei. At this time of urgent flooding, the people of Northern Jiangsu are only preventing them from randomly observing and guiding. The details are recorded as follows:

The Water Level of Weishan Lake Rises Sharply: After the yellow water initially flowed into Nanyang Lake in Southern Shandong, Weishan Lake rose in conjunction. Because the reeds in the two lakes blocked the flow, and the south bank of Nanyang Lake was slightly higher than the north bank, very little water flowed into Weishan Lake. Recently, because the people of Western Shandong were overflowing with Shandong water, they cut down all the reeds in Nanyang Lake, so the downstream was unobstructed. Also, because of the full water in various places in Western Shandong, only Weishan Lake can be injected, so the water level suddenly rose sharply. On the morning of the 29th, it rose sharply by one meter, and then continued to rise. According to yesterday's news, the water head has reached the Sanshui Building in the north of Pei, and is continuing to irrigate from the north bank to the south bank. It is found that the diameter from Nanyang Lake to the south bank of Weishan Lake is 300 li, and the reeds in Weishan Lake are still there, so the south bank is not very tight for the time being, but the north bank has been hit by the disaster. Xia Zhen, on the northeast bank of the lake, belongs to the sixth district of Pei County and is the channel of the waterway. The small embankment that the residents are rushing to block along the lake has been washed away, and the water has risen to the shore, turning the tidal flats into a swamp. Residents on the lake shore are fleeing one after another. Yang Guantun, on the northwest bank of the lake, also belongs to the sixth district of Pei County. The new embankment passes through the area. The water has risen far above the tidal flats, and the water level is half a li away from the embankment at the closest point. Pei City is safe for the time being, but the areas along the lake are in a state of emergency. The Pei County Government sent a clerk Wang to Xuzhou on the 29th to purchase sacks. Peng, the section chief of the Tongshan County Government, handled everything on his behalf. Yesterday, they were transported to Pei by long-distance bus for use in rushing to block the dike. Commissioner Shao is in Pei, supervising the construction of the embankment day and night, which is expected to be completed in about three or four days. It is found that the fifth and sixth breaches at the breach of Linpuji have been washed into one by the water. Although there is no large torrent at present, and the autumn floods have not passed, it is still in danger. If the breaches are not connected, the harm to Northern Jiangsu is far from over.

Representatives from Western Shandong Go to Pei: The people of Western Shandong suspect that the large amount of water flowing into Western Shandong is blocked by the large embankment built in Northern Jiangsu. In fact, the embankment is only built on the west bank of Weishan Lake, a straight embankment running from northwest to southeast, not a horizontal embankment running from east to west. It is still far from the tidal flats of Weishan Lake. Although Weishan Lake has risen several times, the water level has never reached the embankment. This is because the embankment is named the Northern Jiangsu Dike, which caused a misunderstanding. The people of the thirteen counties belonging to Heze recommended Sun Zerang, director of the First Branch of the Shandong Rural Suggestion Research Institute, to come to Xuzhou to conduct an on-site investigation. Sun, who formerly served as the magistrate of Heze County, is very familiar with the situation in Western Shandong. He and two representatives of the people transferred to Kaifeng and came to Xuzhou. After arriving in Xuzhou yesterday morning, he contacted Zhou Xiaoxi, the secretary of the Special Office, and Jian Hua, the secretary of the County Government. He took a bus to Pei to meet Commissioner Shao and asked him to send someone to guide him to inspect the embankment. After inspecting the embankment, Sun and others learned that the function of the embankment was to prevent the lake from overflowing at will, and that it was by no means blocking the water and causing it to flow backward. After the yellow water enters Weishan Lake, if it reaches a certain water level, it can be discharged through the Hulou Shuangzha and Linjiaba in two ways, one directly into the canal and the other around Jingshan in the copper border into the canal. At present, Linjiaba is repairing the embankment and sluice gate, and the Hulou Shuangzha is also planned to be renovated. The Jiangsu Provincial Government will also guide the treatment of the canal to smooth its flow and avoid damage along the way. Sun and others seem to have fully understood this. After the inspection is completed, they will return to Western Shandong to announce and explain to the people to avoid misunderstandings.

Copper Border Dike Project Completed: The Weishan Lake Dike along the copper border has been constructed at an extremely rapid pace since County Magistrate Wang Gongyu led the people to build it at the Wuduan Tuocheng site. Today (31st), it has been fully completed. Wang believed that the people were enthusiastically building the dike, and the township chiefs were supervising the construction. After the embankment was completed, Wang also believed that the embankment and sluice gate of Linjiaba were being repaired, and this gate was the mouth of the south bank of Wei, which was of great importance. If the Wei water level is high, there will be no obstacles to going down the sluice. But if the water force is impacting, it will break the imperial dyke. Therefore, it is planned to build a horizontal dyke in Jing Mountain outside Lanjia Ba to prevent the water force from breaking through horizontally. After the Comfort Conference was opened, the project of repairing the sluice gate at Lanjiaba began immediately. Chief of the Third Section Liu Xinyuan is currently going to supervise the repair, and it is decided to use construction funds to set up an iron plate gate to strengthen it and facilitate the opening and closing of the gate. However, the Hulou Shuangzha project is grand, and the provincial government will send someone to survey it and plan it separately.

All Circles Jointly Telegraph the Provincial Government: Various circles in Xubu telegraphed to the Provincial Government, saying, "Extremely urgent! Chen, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Shen Junjian, Director of the Construction Department, the Yellow River in Shandong burst its banks and flooded south, turning the counties in Southern Shandong into a country of water. Our Ninth District Commissioner Shao and the magistrates of Tong and Pei counties, fearing the arrival of the Yellow River disaster, are conscripting hundreds of thousands of civilians to rush to block the Northern Jiangsu Dike day and night to prevent and control it. And the Yellow River water is coming with great force, and is now rushing straight into Weishan Lake from Nanyang. The lake water has increased by two meters in one day and night. The lake has been silted up for a long time and it is difficult to contain it. If the water level increases by one day, and the big torrent scours the new dike, it is worrying whether it can defend it. It is found that Weishan Lake is a giant reservoir in Jiangbei. If the defense project is not strong, there is a possibility of seizing it and entering the Huai River. Not only will the guiding of the Huai River project fail, but the flooding and submergence of the counties in Northern Jiangsu will be ten times greater than in Southern Shandong. Therefore, we dare to telegraph the Chairman and Director of the Department to personally inspect the dike defense, and instruct how to save the overall situation in Northern Jiangsu. The telegram from Lin is extremely urgent and waiting for orders. Talk Minghua, Standing Committee of the Tongshan County Party Department, Su Qiliu, Construction Committee, and representatives of various groups Li Fengru, Wu Xiaogan, Lan Bohua, Liu Zhiyuan, etc." (July 31)

Devastating Floods in Chaoshan: Han River's White Waves Seal Off Chaozhou City, Turning Coastal Villages into Swamps 82

Shantou Correspondence: The Chaoshan region has been experiencing scorching heat for days. On the 24th evening, the weather suddenly changed, bringing torrential rainfall that continued until the 27th. As a result, the Han River's water level rose dramatically, turning the coast into a marsh. The excessive rainfall in the bordering counties of Fujian and Jiangxi has led to a surge of water flowing downstream to the Chaoshan region, making the Han River the final recipient.

Around Shantou Station on the Chaoshan Railway, over ten *li* from Qishan to Yueqing is submerged. As far as the eye can see, the fields have become lakes and swamps. Fortunately, the early rice harvest was completed, and the autumn rice was just about to be planted, minimizing the losses to the farmers. In the Shuangxi Bridge to Anbu station area, the water level is only four to five feet below the bridge. If it rises further, the trains will have to stop running. In the lower reaches of the Han River, the water flow is rapid. Due to the slippery mud on the embankment, bus services along the levee road were suspended on the 25th. Electric boats traveling from Shantou to Chenghai Donglong were suspended on the 26th due to the dangerous rapid currents. The Chenghai Epu dike, which had previously collapsed due to water erosion, has been repeatedly repaired but remains unstable. Residents from Qishan and Chijiao in the Shantou suburbs are guarding the dike day and night. On the 25th, the dike in Fulong Dongdun village suddenly collapsed, sending water towards Chenghai. The Shantou-Zhangzhou light railway was submerged, slightly easing the water situation in Anbu. Downstream from Anbu station, the fields are mostly filled with yellow, muddy water. Rainwater has accumulated in the fields along the road from Anbu to Chaoan City due to the rising Han River, preventing proper drainage and causing inundation. Citrus fruits, sugarcane, and other agricultural products along the railway have suffered extensive damage from wind and rain, resulting in incalculable losses. Villages along the Han River under the jurisdiction of the Qidu Public Office have also been affected. Strong men are taking turns guarding the dike. Fir wood and sandbags are stockpiled on the dike for emergency rescue. In Chaoan City, the streets and alleys along the West Lake Road and inside the city are filled with accumulated water, creating a desolate scene. Many shops remain closed, and pedestrians wade through the water. Areas like Juying Lane and in front of the county government office are knee-deep in water. At this time, the people inside and outside the city are effectively sealed off by the flood. The east, south, and north city gates, built along the river with sturdy walls, stand over thirty feet tall from the base to the battlements, serving as flood defenses. The terrain outside the city is about six to seven feet to ten feet lower than inside, causing the most hardship for residents outside the walls, who are already submerged in the flood. Whenever the water rises, wooden planks are dropped into the Bamboo Gate, Upper Water Gate, and Lower Water Gate of Chaozhou City to prevent water from entering. Each plank is eight inches high and fourteen feet long, matching the size of the city gate. After the first layer of planks is in place, the second layer of planks inside the city is also prepared in case the water breaches the first layer, providing a second line of defense. Sandbags are placed behind the planks. On the 26th, fifteen planks were lowered, with the water reaching the eighth plank, about six feet above ground level. Without the city walls, Chaoan City would be completely flooded. The embankment stretches over fifty thousand feet and stands five *zhang* above the land, but the riverbed has been silted up with mud and sand over the years, making the river bottom higher than the land inside the embankment. If the embankment were to collapse, the Han River could change its course and flow into the sea from Jieyang. Chaoan, Chenghai, and Jieyang counties would be the first to suffer damage. Therefore, during days of high water levels, the eighteen floating bridge boats in the middle of the surging waves were unmoored. Each of the twenty-four large bridge piles, which originally had two to four shops on them, now only has the corners of the roofs above the water. The sound of the water washing them away is deafening, and the entire bridge is submerged. Only whirlpools mark the location of the bridge piles. Further away, only tree branches above the water are visible. It is reported that many places along the river have become swamps, but thankfully, there have been no reports of dike collapses. The current in the river is swift, and the distance between the two banks is about ten *li*. A few ferries provide transportation, but fares are very expensive. People walk slowly. Zhumenzhijie Street, which leads to the river, is like a stream or river. The tall waterfront wharves cannot operate due to the high water. Boats are moored on the uneven city wall, creating a natural dock. Outside the Zhumen Gate, the shops and houses are mostly inhabited by poor people and are very small. Poor men, women, and children huddle on the tiled roofs, eating, resting, and sleeping on the uneven tiles, using umbrellas to shield themselves from the wind and rain, looking pathetic. Some women and children squat and wail, creating a truly miserable scene.

The Tragic Robbery Cases in Songjiang and Punan

Lu Yunlian, head of the Seventh Bao of the Nineteenth Tu of the Seventh District of Punan, was robbed. She is the head of the seventh bao. She returned home the night before last after working in Songjiang. That night, more than ten robbers suddenly broke into her home and robbed her. The robbers found gun bullets and demanded the location of the firearm, even using fire to burn her. Eventually, they stole a self-defense pistol with the county seal No. 274 and more than thirty rifle bullets. They also took fox and sheepskin robes, gold and pearl jewelry, resulting in significant losses. Also, the home of Jiang Siquan, the third household of the second Jia of the second Bao of Xihutang Township in the Eighth District, was attacked by more than ten robbers at one o'clock in the morning on the 30th. They broke down the door and entered. The victim and his nephew, A Mao, stepped forward to resist but were beaten with wooden sticks. Jiang Siquan and A Mao were severely beaten. The robbers stole three *dan* of white rice, four pieces of clothing, five yuan in banknotes, six bolts of cloth, and nine sacks before fleeing. The County Public Security Bureau received a long-distance telephone report from the Ninth Sub-Bureau Director that Jiang Siquan suffered chest injuries from the robbery and had died from his injuries before he could be treated. His nephew, A Mao, also sustained serious leg injuries.

Ying Shi, the President of the Wuxian District Court, was ordered to exchange positions with Lu Yimei, the President of the Jinan District Court. Mr. Lu arrived in Suzhou from Jinan the day before yesterday. After meeting with President Ying, he officially took office at the Wu District Court at 10:00 AM yesterday (the 1st). Wuxi: Labor unrest at Zhenxin Yarn Factory flares up again

The Zhenxin Yarn Factory in Taibaodun, outside the West Gate, experienced a strike on May 17th. Some people were injured and property was damaged. Workers wages were withheld. Up to the present, four wage periods are owed to workers. On the morning of the 31st, the families of the workers, twenty three in total, requested payment from the factory due to difficult living conditions. The factory agreed to pay forty dollars to each family and two dollars per mother, as a temporary solution. However, the factory's wage payments, were scheduled to be paid from the 9th to the 25th of each month, totaling over ten thousand yuan. The factory has not yet paid the wages for July. The workers repeatedly demanded payment from the factory, but the factory insisted on postponing payment until August 15th. The workers refused and began a work stoppage at 4:00 PM. That night, representatives of the factory's branch labor union, Wu Zhenxiang, Liu Borong, You Quangen, and others, led more than four hundred day-shift workers to the County Party Headquarters to petition. Xiao Ruoqian met with them and advised the workers to return first and wait for the County Government to convene representatives from both labor and management for mediation. The workers were satisfied with this. However, the manager, Jiang Shiqing, avoided meeting with them, forcing them to wait outside the door, sleepless and unfed, in a pathetic state. The remaining thousand night-shift workers gathered in the factory square, maintaining order. The heads of the First and Fourth Public Security Bureaus sent police to suppress the unrest. The situation calmed down yesterday morning, and the dispute was resolved. However, the factory is facing tight credit due to the high price of cotton and low price of yarn, and may temporarily suspend operations.

Changshu: Three Male and Female Corpses Discovered in Hengjing Pond

On the morning of the 31st, three male and female bodies were discovered in the Hengjing Pond along the Shanghai-Nanjing Highway outside Xiaodongmen in our county. One man was found embracing a woman, not separating even in death, creating a peculiar sight. The news spread quickly, drawing crowds of onlookers. The village police reported the incident to the Public Security Branch, which in turn reported it to the County Government. Investigator He Cheng was dispatched to the village to examine the bodies. Since there were no family members present, the police station launched an investigation to identify the deceased and determine the cause of death. The village police then collected the bodies for burial.

The opening ceremony of Jiangsu Province Children's Year was held at 8:00 AM on the 1st in the auditorium of the Provincial Party Headquarters. About thirty elementary schools, with over a thousand children participating. Director of Education Zhou Fohai presided over the ceremony and delivered a speech on the significance of Children's Year. Ningbo: Five Native Banks Collapse on the Same Day

The native banks in this city have always been known for their reliability. At the end of last month, as financial turmoil tightened in Shanghai, the Ningbo native banks were not affected because of their strong financial standing. Unexpectedly, at the end of this month, five banks including Da Tong Hengyuan, Xinyuan, Yongyuan, Taiyuan, and Wuyuan all declared liquidation on the same day, representing an unprecedented blow to the local banking industry. Hengyuan Bank, which had been in operation for over twenty years, had a capital of 33,000 yuan, with total annual receipts and payments reaching 1,000 yuan. The amount for receipts and payments was approximately 700,000, with deposits of 400,000 yuan and loans of approximately 1 million yuan. It owed 130,000 yuan to public banks. Yongyuan Bank had a capital of 27,500 yuan, an attached capital of 17,500 yuan, and annual receipts and payments of approximately 1 million yuan. After offsetting debts, there was still a surplus of over 100,000 yuan. Taiyuan Bank had a capital of 50,000 yuan, with total annual receipts and payments of approximately 1 million yuan. Wuyuan Bank had a capital of 50,000 yuan, an attached capital of 50,000 yuan, and total annual receipts and payments of approximately 500,000 yuan, deposits of 130,000 yuan. After offsetting various transactions, there was still a surplus of over 10,000 yuan. Huida, an exchange house, also declared liquidation through a lawyer due to financial difficulties. The Bankers Association urgently convened a meeting yesterday to discuss the situation.

Local News

American Railroad Magnate Mr. Bernadet Arrives in Shanghai for a Tour. He States That This Is His First Visit. He Will Leave Shanghai Tomorrow Morning to Return Home. 83

American railroad authority Mr. Bernadet arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday with his wife for a leisurely tour. Mr. Bernadet is an American railroad magnate whose railroad operations exceed the total length of railroads in our entire country. A Central News Agency reporter visited him yesterday and learned the following details:

First Visit to the Far East

Mr. Bernadet first stated that he and his wife are taking advantage of the summer vacation to tour the Far East. They departed from San Francisco by ship on the 2nd of last month, first arriving in Yokohama, Japan, then touring major Japanese cities. They then went to Korea, passing through the three northeastern provinces before arriving in Shanghai by train from Beiping. This is his first visit to the Far East, but it is a whirlwind tour with insufficient time to stay. The countries of East Asia are all making great progress, and their railroad industries are also developing. He met with railroad leaders from both China and Japan, but he has no other missions here besides touring and observing.

Glimpses of Operations

The railroads he operates total 13,500 miles, connecting California, Mexico, Chicago, San Francisco, Illinois, Ohio, Minnesota, Virginia, Florida, and other places. The headquarters are in Chicago. There are currently 316 passenger cars, 200 of which are sleeping cars. He began operating railroads in Indian Territory in 1895. He is old now, but is determined to continue working until he is satisfied before retiring.

Opinions on Developing Transportation

Mr. Bernadet believes that transportation development should be promoted by land, sea, and air in coordination. He also stated that trains are convenient for transportation and mentioned that American airline companies also operate railroads, showing that transportation development should be complementary. China's railroad industry has been progressing since the end of the European War, but much more effort is still needed.

Leaving Shanghai Tomorrow Morning to Return Home

Mr. Bernadet concluded that his company's economic situation has been unremarkable in recent years. A large portion of the railway is used to pay for taxes and operating expenses. While there is some profit, it is only enough to cover expenses. A small portion is profitable, but those funds are used for equipment and development. He has decided to take the Chichibu Maru to Japan and return to his duties, as his vacation is over. The ship is scheduled to depart from Shanghai tomorrow morning at 5:00 AM.

Swiss National Day Celebrated Yesterday. Swiss Officials and Residents in Shanghai Celebrate Together. 84

Yesterday was Swiss National Day. Swiss officials and residents in Shanghai all took a holiday to celebrate. Industrial and Commercial Loans Implemented Yesterday; General League of National Products Discusses Fundamental Solutions 85

The Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee's 20 million yuan relief loan program was implemented yesterday. The General League of National Products Committee held a membership meeting to discuss fundamental solutions. Details are as follows:

Relief Loans Begin Yesterday: The Ministry of Finance allocated 20 million yuan in national treasury bonds, establishing the Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee to manage them and administer the relief loans. (1) The total amount for small credit loans is limited to 5 million yuan. Over 1,500 application forms have been requested after the City Chamber of Commerce forwarded them. However, only a few have been completed and submitted to the committee for review. The committee has decided to first dispatch specialists to investigate the two joint liability firms listed on the forms and the assets of the borrowers before submitting them to the committee for review and approval, and then notifying them of payment. (2) The total amount for mortgage loans is limited to 15 million yuan. Factories and trading firms are independently negotiating. After reaching an agreement, they will submit the applications to the committee for review. If approved, national treasury bonds will be issued as secondary collateral.

National Products Groups Meeting for Discussion: The General League of National Products Committee held its 50th regular meeting yesterday. They discussed fundamental solutions for rescuing industry and commerce. In addition to the representatives who had previously contacted the loan committee reporting on the progress and the Ministry of Finance's approval, the committee also proposed issuing public bonds to stabilize the financial market and providing loans to rescue industry and commerce. However, those were deemed only as temporary measures. The fundamental solution, according to the committee, would be to find an alternative to cash and reform the currency system by having the government issue paper money backed by goods, which would allow for the concentration of cash for national defense and construction. Therefore, they expressed support for the recently published "Theory of Currency Reform" by Chu Huiseng and decided to distribute it to member factories of the national products organizations for detailed study and response within a specified period of time, before further consideration.

City Chamber of Commerce Begins Exchanging Old Revenue Stamps Yesterday; Handling in Conjunction with the Provincial Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau; Old Stamps Worth Over 20,000 Yuan to be Exchanged in Three Months 86

After the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce received the Ministry of Finance's order to issue six regulations for exchanging old revenue stamps, it established an Office for Verification and Exchange of Revenue Stamps, located at the lower level of the Chamber of Commerce at the Tianhou Palace Bridge. Starting yesterday, it dispatched personnel to work with personnel from the Provincial Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau to begin the verification and exchange process. All those who registered old revenue stamps with the Chamber of Commerce last year can submit the registered old revenue stamps to the office, where they will be verified, sealed, and stored for exchange for new stamps. Office hours are from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM every day except holidays. A reporter from the New Voice News learned that the old revenue stamps registered in Shanghai are worth approximately 30,000 yuan. According to the regulations, "Those with 20,000 to 40,000 [yuan] will be exchanged evenly over three months."

City Finance Bureau Begins Collecting Autumn Property Tax Yesterday; Limited to Fifteen Days for Self-Submission and Payment 87

The City Finance Bureau began collecting the autumn property tax yesterday. According to the announcement issued by the bureau, after improving the property tax collection method in the city starting this summer, the bureau issued an announcement. Collection for the autumn property tax this year is scheduled to begin on August 1st. For those with a tax amount of over ten yuan, the bureau will issue a notice during the collection period, limiting taxpayers to self-submit and pay within fifteen days. Those who fail to pay within ten days after the deadline will be subject to an on-site collection by bureau staff with a fine of two percent of the tax amount. Those with a tax amount of less than ten yuan will still be collected by bureau staff. Those who voluntarily submit and pay the tax are welcome to do so. South City Collection Office: No. 29 Maojia Lane, South Shanghai; West City Collection Office: No. 501 Rue Robert, West Shanghai; North City Collection Office: No. 110 Datong Road, Zhabei.

Eurasia Company Pioneers New Shaanxi-Chengdu Route; Test Flight Yesterday Morning; Departed at 8:40 AM and Arrived in Xi'an in the Afternoon; To Test Fly from Shaanxi to Hanzhong and Then to Chengdu This Morning 88

In order to facilitate transportation between Sichuan and Shaanxi, the Ministry of Communications specially ordered the Shanghai Eurasia Aviation Corporation to pioneer a new Shaanxi-Chengdu air route last month. After receiving the order, the company's general manager, Li Jingzong, began active preparations and personally inspected the route from Pingliang to Shaanxi last week. After returning to Shanghai, he prepared for the test flight. Now that everything is ready, the company's deputy head of the aviation group, He En'er, Xi'an station director Yang Xingzhong, and pilot Count Pastell, flew a Junkers 34 large aircraft from Longhua Airport at 8:40 AM yesterday to test the entire route. Mr. Li Jingzong originally planned to accompany the flight and inspect the route along the way, but he cancelled his plan due to many important public affairs in Shanghai.

Arrived in Xi'an After 4:00 PM: A reporter from the Huadong News Agency inquired with a company representative at 6:00 PM yesterday, who said that the test flight took off from Longhua Airport at 8:40 AM. The weather was favorable yesterday, making the test flight very smooth. The aircraft was equipped with radio communication equipment and had been reporting its location to Shanghai via telegraph along the way. It passed the capital at 10:05 AM, Zhengzhou at 1:10 PM, and arrived at Xi'an Airport at 4:31 PM, arriving 59 minutes earlier than previous flights, setting a new record.

Overnight in Xi'an, Flying to Chengdu This Morning: According to the company's Secretary Cha, the company already had a route from Luoyang to Xi'an, making the test flight relatively simple. The distance was 1,290 kilometers. However, the company did not have a route from Xi'an to Chengdu, making the test flight more difficult. The distance is unknown due to the lack of test flights, but it is estimated to be around 600 kilometers. The route is mountainous. If the test flight goes smoothly, it will take three hours to complete. The test flight aircraft that departed yesterday will stay overnight in Xi'an and will test fly from Xi'an via Hanzhong to Chengdu at 8:00 AM this morning without stopping.

No Definite News on Formal Opening: The reporter from the Huadong News Agency inquired about the formal launch date after this test flight. According to Secretary Cha, it was rumored the outside had already decided to launch the route on the tenth of this month, but the company would postpone that date if the preparations fell behind.
