The Postal and Remittance Bureau Supervisory Committee Established Yesterday; All Supervisors Simultaneously Took Office...Then Held the First Meeting 94

According to the Central News Agency, the Supervisory Committee of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau was established yesterday morning. The supervisors arrived at the bureau to take office, without holding a ceremony. They then held their first meeting. The Ministry of Communications sent Vice Minister Zhang Daofan to attend and provide guidance. During the meeting, they discussed and passed the procedural rules and the next meeting date, adjourning at noon. The details are recorded below.

Supervisors Take Office: The supervisors who took office at the bureau yesterday were Song Ziliang, Lin Jinyu, Shen Zao, Wu Dajun, Fen, Wang Xiang, Qian Xinzhi, Zhou Pei, and eight others. Huang Zongxiao did not participate due to being abroad. After the supervisors arrived at the bureau, Director Shen Shuyu and others received them in the office to rest. At that time, banking leaders Chen Jian'an, Bei Songsheng, Shen Qing, Qu Jigang, Gu Yigu, Xi Demao, Rao Taoshu, and Zhang Peishen went to offer congratulations, led by Song.

First Meeting: After the supervisors took office, the first meeting was held in the Supervisory Committee room. In addition to the supervisors, the Ministry of Communications sent Vice Minister Zhang Daofan to attend and provide guidance. Postal and Remittance Bureau Director Shen Shuyu and Deputy Director Zhou Shouliang also attended. The meeting recorded the procedural rules and decided to hold the next meeting on September 6th, adjourning at noon. The committee has submitted a document to the Ministry of Communications reporting the process of taking office and holding the first meeting.

Vice Minister Gives Instructions: Vice Minister Zhang delivered an instruction, saying, "I am honored to have been ordered to attend this grand meeting. The Supervisory Committee has a long history before its organization. It was discussed when the Postal Economic System Research Committee was established in the 20th year of the Republic. Recently, the government formulated the organization. The members are leaders in the industrial, commercial, auditing, and accounting fields. Under your guidance and supervision, the savings and remittance business will surely achieve greater results and contribute to the country. However, the savings and remittance business is of great importance to the national economy and should not be aimed at ordinary business methods. Even from the perspective of the savings business alone, our country currently has only over 40 million yuan in savings, which is far behind England and Japan. There is much that needs to be designated and promoted by the members. Today, Minister Zhu is unable to attend due to official business and has asked me to express his gratitude to you and hopes for more guidance and strict exercise of supervisory powers."

Committee Chairman's Speech: Chairman Song delivered an opening speech, saying, "This committee was included in the organizational law at the beginning of the establishment of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau as a special bureau. Due to personnel changes, it has not been realized for a long time. For several years, the savings and remittance business has achieved remarkable results and made daily progress due to the strong position and credibility of the post office and the planning and management of previous authorities. Minister Zhu believes that it is necessary to establish this committee, so he entrusted it to the colleagues of the conference. This committee is officially established today. Although I feel that my talents are limited and the task is heavy, because the savings and remittance business is state-owned and closely related to society and the people, I cannot refuse. I plan to do my best to follow you and collect ideas to benefit the public and contribute to the people. The post office has been operating savings for sixteen years and has improved several times. The savings bureau has expanded to more than 640 branches, and the total amount of savings has reached more than 42.2 million yuan, which can be said to be progress. However, based on the national population, each person saves only one jiao (1/10 of a yuan), which is far behind the average savings of 70 yuan per person in the United Kingdom and 50 yuan per person in Japan. Even in terms of savings, compared with the amount of savings in foreign-run savings institutions in China, we are far behind. Moreover, in terms of percentage, urban savings account for 70%, while rural areas account for only 30%, which is an abnormal development. This is not due to poor planning, but simply because the percentage of rural savings in our country can make rapid progress. The remittance business was established even earlier, but it has not made significant progress in 30 years. According to the statistics of the 22nd year of the Republic, the total amount of remittances was approximately 17.5 million yuan. Although the exchange rate has been reduced, the amount of remittances has not increased sharply. Although there are more and more banks, and all of them are engaged in remittance business, the fees are low, and the procedures are simple, it seems that the savings and remittance bureau is difficult to compete with. In fact, the nature of postal savings and remittance is different from that of ordinary banks. Ordinary banks mostly operate commercial savings and commercial remittances, while postal savings and remittance serve the common people in remote rural areas. Most of our country's banks are located in cities, while rural towns are often absent. As for post offices, they penetrate into the people and are everywhere. It seems that we should use this point to encourage the savings of small people as much as possible and store and transport them to various national construction projects. All countries use savings deposits, and postal savings are one of the sources of funds. Our country has many things to be done and is just in its infancy, so it is difficult to compare. However, if we determine the direction and put the funds into reliable public construction projects and industrial and commercial industries, if we can implement it properly, the development of transportation, the relief of rural decline, and the prosperity of industry and commerce will surely benefit greatly. But on the other hand, we must be especially cautious about the use of funds, because postal savings and remittances are mostly the hard-earned money of the working people, accumulated bit by bit through saving and frugality. This type of savings should be given the greatest possible protection to avoid any loss, so that the public will have a deeper faith in postal savings, which will also encourage people to save. The mission of this committee is extremely important. In terms of responsibility, it is not only responsible to the government, but also to the people who deposit savings, so that the savings and remittance bureau takes the interests of the people and uses appropriate methods to apply it to the people. The greatest mission of the savings and remittance business is to seek welfare for the people, not just to make profits. The postal savings and remittance business has achieved remarkable results since the establishment of the special bureau. At present, Director Shen, Deputy Director Zhou, and the colleagues in the bureau are making every effort to operate and regulate the bureau, and the future development is immeasurable. This is indeed a very fortunate thing. Today, this committee is established, which happens to be in the hot summer. We are grateful to Minister Zhu for sending Representative Zhang Daofan to participate and guide, and colleagues from afar have come to participate in the ceremony. I am very happy. I am not well-versed in scholarship, and I am willing to follow you and encourage each other to live up to the government's appointment and the expectations of the people who deposit savings."

For the sake of unifying the organization of civilian shipping industry groups, the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, in accordance with the Supplementary Measures for the Organization of Shipping Merchants promulgated by the National Government and the interpretation regulations of the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee, after repeated consultations and careful consideration, issued Order No. 80 yesterday, appointing Xu Hanzhang, Feng Qingyu, Zhu Tongfu, Xiang Runsheng, Yuan Jingen, Feng Jinbiao, Yu Limin, Yang Jincan, Yu Jihai, Peng Debiao, Cao Yuyu, Zhu Ziqian, Peng Guinian, Wu Shungui, and Yu Fuyun as preparatory members of the Shanghai Civilian Shipping Industry Association, and designated Xu Hanzhang as the convener of the first preparatory meeting, to start preparing immediately. The Insurance Society Will Be Established Tomorrow 98

The Chinese Insurance Society was first initiated by Mr. Luo Beichen, manager of the Wuhan District of the Life Insurance Department of the China Insurance Company, and others in Hankou. After three months of preparation, it began to take shape. In early July, Mr. Luo came to Shanghai and, after more than ten days of effort, invited dozens of people, including Song Hanzhang, Zhang Mingxin, Ding Xuernong, Lu Yuequan, Liang Chenlan, Hu Yongqi, Zhu Rutang, Xu Kesheng, Wang Xiaowen, and Zhang Sumin, to participate in the initiation. The inaugural meeting is scheduled to be held tomorrow (3rd) at 4:00 PM at the Hua An Building on the second floor. The origins and the inaugural meeting notice are as follows:

Origins: Theory is the guide of facts, and facts are the evidence of theory. This is undeniable. Therefore, with a new theory, the old environment will always be transformed and new theories will be produced. The two are mutually causal, because theory without facts is empty talk, and facts without theory are difficult to exemplify. People in Europe, America, and Japan understand this principle very well. In their countries, scholars and entrepreneurs always communicate and work together, organizing various societies for joint research, so that all careers and academics can move forward along a certain right track. Our country lags behind in everything. Fortunately, in recent years, we have gradually begun to transform various emerging social undertakings, exploring principles and building realities. The number of great scholars and entrepreneurs is gradually increasing, but scholars are scholars, and entrepreneurs are entrepreneurs. Theory and facts are often incompatible, or even go in opposite directions. It is not easy to get the two to complement each other. This is the main reason why our country's facts cannot progress rapidly. Now, taking the insurance industry as an example, through the mutual efforts of scholars and entrepreneurs in Europe and the United States, the general public has deeply realized that the insurance industry is a perfect economic organization, a mutual social service, a national strategy for establishing oneself and others, and a financial system with solid assets. Therefore, the insurance industry is booming and has grasped the world's great economic authority and established a solid foundation for people's livelihood. Our country's insurance industry has also made considerable progress, but it is still far behind Europe and the United States. When our country's national economy is bankrupt and national construction is backward, we deeply feel that the insurance industry has the need to rise up and take on the responsibility of reversing the situation. Because the insurance industry is a stabilizing technique, transforming the real environment, and establishing the country's permanent economic security. We hope that scholars and insurance entrepreneurs will enthusiastically participate and work hard to make the society flourish and promote the success of the national economic construction movement. This is what we sincerely pray for. Initiators: Song Hanzhang, Zhang Minghuang, Gong Xuernong, Lu Yuequan, Liang Chenlan, Xu Kesheng, Wang Xiaowen, Wei Beichen.

Notice: Dear Sir/Madam, the Chinese Insurance Society is now ready for establishment. It is hereby scheduled to hold the inaugural meeting at 4:00 PM on Saturday, August 3rd (this Saturday) at the Hua An Building on Jing'an Temple Road. Please arrive on time to celebrate the grand occasion. Sincerely, the Preparatory Office of the Chinese Insurance Society.

Hu Wenhu Donates Medicine for Disaster Relief 100

Mr. Hu's concern for the disaster victims is meticulous and admirable. The municipal government plans to distribute the above-mentioned medicines to various disaster areas as soon as they arrive.

The Taxpayers' Association Re-requests the Municipal Council to Collect General Rates Based on Actual Rent 101

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Settlement wrote to the Municipal Council, stating, "Dear Sirs, according to a letter from lawyer Cai Guangxu, 'Our client, the Guoxin Bank, leased two ground-floor rooms in the south of the Securities Building at No. 422 Hankou Road from the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange in March of this year as its business address, stipulating a monthly rent of 800 silver dollars, or 9,600 yuan per year, and paying property rates (commonly known as police rates) at 14%, which should be 112 silver dollars per month, or 1,344 yuan per year. Unexpectedly, the Municipal Council's Rates Office did not collect rates according to the actual rent, but insisted on estimating and raising the value to 16,000 yuan per year, requiring a monthly payment of 186.66 yuan, or 2,242 yuan per year, which is almost double the actual rent. Our client naturally could not agree to this according to the law. After discussing with them, there was no effect. Our lawyer then consulted with Mr. Bourne, the director of the Rates Office, several times, and he once agreed to reduce the estimated value of 16,000 yuan by 20% (i.e., to 12,800 yuan), but our client believed that this violated the law and could not accept it. Then, our lawyer sent a written statement to the Municipal Council, stating that this dispute could be resolved by the court, but the Council ignored it and instead sent a letter stating that the case had been sent to the Property Rates Assessment Committee for review. Unexpectedly, on July 11th, we received a letter from Mr. Phillips, acting secretary-general of the Council, stating that the committee had assessed the rent of the Guoxin Bank at 17,000 yuan per year. After reading this, we were shocked. Afterwards, our lawyer went to the Municipal Council's Rates Office to inquire about this method and the reasons for the decision, but was told that the assessment of the committee did not announce the reasons. In the future, if the Guoxin Bank resists the rates, they will have other methods to enforce them without requesting the court. However, in order to save the bank's face, they may report to senior officials (referring to the secretary-general) that due to the current economic downturn, the rates will be collected at the original rate of 16,000 yuan for the time being, and the full amount will be collected when business gradually improves. Our client has several doubts about this method of the Municipal Council, which we will try to explain to your Council: (1) The Property Rates Assessment Committee is neither an independent body nor recognized by our Chinese Ratepayers' Association. The committee is actually under the direction and payroll of the Municipal Council. Its nature is merely an advisor to the Council. No taxpayer in the settlement should be bound by it, especially since the assessment does not include reasons, which obviously lacks a legal basis; (2) The Municipal Council collects property rates, except for self-owned property, which is calculated at 14% of the actual rent. Now, it is forcibly estimating the value for our client, exceeding the regulations by almost double, which is undoubtedly arbitrary and excessive; (3) The amount of the value is based on a certain object (movable and immovable property), and the value is determined by both the seller or lessor and the buyer or lessee. There is a transaction, and there is also a market price. The Guoxin Bank's address has been vacant for more than two years since its completion, and no one has consulted it. During this period, it can be said that there is no value standard. Now, our client leases it from the landlord at a monthly rent of 800 yuan, which is the standard value of this address. Both parties have a contract, and there are rent receipts and account books for reference. If there is an intention to take profits outside the law in order to reduce property rates, our client is willing to be punished according to the law; (4) The Municipal Council has issued notices and distributed forms to all landlords and property management offices to investigate the actual amount of rent as the standard for collecting property rates. Therefore, the Municipal Council's collection of rates should be based on rent, which is undoubtedly true; (5) The Council even said that it has other methods to enforce it, which is nothing more than stopping the supply of water and electricity. Regardless of whether this method is legal, the public utilities that serve the public interest are used as weapons by the Council to oppress taxpayers, which also violates the public opinion of taxpayers. If it is implemented, the losses suffered by our client as a result should be borne by the Council. The above points are all that we cannot refrain from saying. This Council's increase in the assessment of rent and the increase in the collection of property rates, which exceeds 24% of what should be paid, is shocking. If we do not find a way to stop it, not only will the Council use it as an example in the future, but it will gradually increase property rates for other Chinese and foreign residents, and even the owners will increase rents based on the Council's assessment. Once this trend starts, disputes will arise repeatedly. In this autumn of declining industries and impoverishment of the people, how can we bear the burden of repeated oppression, or incidents may occur as a result, and the consequences may be difficult to deal with. This is not just a matter of concern for our client. Therefore, we hereby report to your Council, requesting your Council to seriously negotiate with the Municipal Council to cancel the illegal increase in rates.' After the above situation was reported to the Council, the Council found that the collection of municipal general rates without following the actual rent has been repeatedly corrected by the Council. If your Council, for the sake of the taxpayers, considers the number of rents estimated by the land price regulations to be lower than the market price (i.e., the actual rent), and this was done more than ten years ago, although the Council believes that it should collect rates based on the actual rent according to law and reason, it does not object to your Council's benevolent governance. However, now, without collecting rates based on the actual rent, you want to overestimate the rent in order to increase the rates, which means that your Council is only considering financial interests and disregarding law and reason, which the Council finds very regrettable. The Council saw several years ago that the Shanghai market would inevitably decline day by day, and the number of vacant houses would inevitably increase day by day. It sent a letter requesting your Council to make changes to its financial plan to avoid becoming a sequel to Chicago. In order to reduce the expenses of the useless and unprofitable music team for the vast majority of taxpayers, the Council also considered the financial situation of your Council and resolved at the Congress in the 13th year of the Republic of China that 'general rates should be collected for vacant houses,' as the regulations on the land of the Yangjingbang do not prohibit the collection of general rates for vacant houses, just as land must also be taxed. However, your Council does not implement this, and it must overestimate the rent for the general rates that have actual rent in order to increase it. Is it necessary to make the houses rented by the few remaining businesses become the houses of Hardoon Yanghang on Nanjing Road and Pingzhiming Yanghang on Hankou Road and make taxes protect them? As for the Valuation Committee, it wastes taxpayers' taxes and has no basis in fundamental law. In the opinion of the taxpayers, it is equal to a court's judgment. The issue of authority is very serious and should be given special consideration by your Council. According to the letter, please send a letter to your Council as soon as possible, unless there is a notarized report, to collect the general rates of the Guoxin Bank according to the actual rent."

Various Charity Groups Receive Pleas for Aid 102

News from the Sino-Foreign Relief Committee: (A) Chairman Han of Jinan Replied: "To the esteemed Sino-Foreign Relief Committee, your telegram of the 30th has been received. The Yellow River has burst its banks, causing widespread flooding and disaster. Starving refugees cry out across the desolate landscape. We are deeply grateful that the Daode Society Relief Group has not abandoned us and has come to Shandong to provide relief. Our government and all the affected people are profoundly moved. We will follow your instructions and provide sincere hospitality. Please convey our heartfelt thanks. Day and night, until the afternoon of the 7th, the water depth on the plains reached four to five feet. The next day, mountain floods erupted, and the Dan and Xi Rivers surged simultaneously, rushing violently. The water level rose to over twenty feet. Furthermore, due to the narrow mountain rivers downstream and poor communication, the water accumulated higher and higher, eventually engulfing mountains and hills, creating a boundless expanse. Within our county, from Xizhen in the west to Liguanqiao in the east, a total distance of over one hundred *li* (approximately 30 miles) became a vast ocean, turning into a state of flooding. Residents either clung to trees, wooden houses, or fled to the mountains. Those who were old or weak and unable to escape were swept away with their homes, livestock, and food. In total, over one hundred villages in the county were affected, with none spared. Among them, Zhangzhuang, Wangying, Shuanghezhen, and over one hundred other towns suffered particularly severe inundation, with former dwellings transformed into raging torrents. In Liguanqiao Town, the flood breached the walls, and the water depth inside the walls exceeded ten feet, resulting in the deaths of no less than four thousand people. In areas such as Bating, hailstorms occurred simultaneously, killing trees, injuring people and livestock, and the situation is beyond description. The water depth in the city reached five to six feet, and most of the houses collapsed. The county government only has a dozen or so remaining civilian houses. As one can imagine, the current water level has slightly decreased, but all the people in the county are on the verge of starvation and death. The cries of the afflicted fill the land, a scene of unparalleled devastation, causing heartache and tears. In addition to submitting a request to various organizations in the province for immediate relief, we are sending this special telegram to implore you to provide generous aid." (B) A telegram from Wang Shiliu, the Sixth District Administrative Director of Hubei Province, states: "Investigations reveal that continuous rain has caused a disaster, with the Xiang River rising sharply and floods reaching thirty to forty feet, turning the plains into swamps. Guanghua, Gucheng, Xiangyang, Yicheng, and other counties along the river have suffered severely from the floods. Ripening crops have been completely submerged, and countless lives have been transformed into fish and shrimp. The cities and towns of Laohekou and Fancheng, known as the commercial centers of northern Hubei, have seen more than half of their houses collapse, and goods have been completely washed away. The devastation is unprecedented. Although the floods have subsided, countless displaced persons are without clothing or food. In Fancheng alone, there are still over thirty thousand people. The situation elsewhere can be imagined. The cries of the starving fill the land, awaiting immediate assistance. We are sending this special telegram to appeal for urgent relief to save the dying people."

Enthusiastic Donations from All Sectors. Upon hearing the news of the floods in the Yellow River and Yangtze River regions, various sectors at home and abroad have automatically donated funds for relief, which have been remitted to the committee for distribution. This demonstrates a warm spirit of charity. Furthermore, Zhou Hongen of Anhui County wrote a letter stating: "Respectfully, due to the bandit Sun's attack on Bozhou in October of the 14th year of the Republic (1925), the entire city was in difficulty. Fortunately, the Sino-Foreign Relief Committee, the Relief Association, and the World Red Swastika Society, organized by various philanthropists, and the Yuan Daoyin, who presided over the temporary emergency relief efforts, rescued the people, allowing them to survive and the dead to be buried. At that time, I received five yuan in relief funds from your organization to bury my late father. I am deeply grateful. Now, I am sending ten yuan via the post office to be allocated to the severely affected disaster areas to save the survivors."

China Relief Society. We have recently received a report from Zhang Lanfen, chairman of the embankment engineering committee of Huaining County, and committee member Song Shancheng, and others, stating that in the Hushan Township area of the First District of Huaining County, Anhui Province, from Majiadian, Laohuta, Zhujiadun, Shuanghekou, Jiangjiadian, Liushulin, Jijiadun, Changbujia, and other places, totaling thirty *li* (approximately 9 miles) along the river, ten large and small embankments have been breached by violent tides since the beginning of last month until the end of the month. The people, who had already suffered greatly from last year's drought, made extraordinary efforts to repair the embankments, working day and night, but were unable to prevent the breaches. The loss of embankment materials is estimated to be over ten thousand yuan. The embankments have still collapsed, resulting in widespread flooding, inundating countless fields and houses, and carrying away people, livestock, and coffins in uncountable numbers. There is not a single dry spot within the flooded area. The affected people are climbing onto roofs and trees for temporary shelter. Last year there was a drought, and this year there is flooding, disaster upon disaster, an unprecedented occurrence. This has led to the tragedy of the young and strong fleeing, and the old and weak perishing in ditches. Currently, the affected people are unable to get a full meal every day and are desperately hoping for relief. We are sending a special telegram to implore you to provide generous assistance, quickly allocate large sums of money, and send personnel to provide relief to save the remaining survivors." According to previous reports, the disasters in Hubei, Henan, and Shandong provinces are severe. Many embankments in Anhui Province have been breached and urgently need rescue. In previous years, the society has spent no less than hundreds of thousands of yuan on relief efforts in various counties of Anhui, including Yi, Wu, Anqing, and northern Anhui. Now, another severe flood has occurred. It is hoped that benevolent compatriots will generously donate to save these helpless survivors.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Businesses to Promote Domestically Produced Cigarettes; Only These Are to be Purchased for Customers 103

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday notified various trade guilds, stating: "Respectfully, we received a letter from the Chinese National Cigarette Maintenance Association on the 30th of this month stating: 'In recent years, the business of domestically produced cigarettes has been declining day by day. The association, as a pioneer in promoting domestic products and a driving force in protecting domestic industries, was officially established on the 19th of this month and has been guided by your esteemed chamber. However, this matter is of great importance and involves many aspects. It relies on collective wisdom and effort to overcome difficulties. It is hoped that you will inform your respective member guilds to rise up together and work together to maintain the domestic cigarette industry, so that the future of domestic products will become brighter and more prosperous. The beneficiaries will not only be the domestic cigarette industry.' The chamber has instructed the personnel in charge of purchasing cigarettes for customers to only purchase domestic products, and this has been implemented for many years. As the saying goes, 'A journey of a thousand miles begins with a single step.' This is not difficult to achieve. If the chairmen and standing committee members of various guilds can sincerely instruct their personnel to only purchase domestic cigarettes for customers and pay close attention to this matter at all times, and if there are any violations, they should be instructed to make a change, and if they themselves set an example by only smoking domestic cigarettes, then the trend will change imperceptibly and spread to all members of the industry. In the future, whenever various guilds hold general membership meetings and the chamber sends personnel to provide guidance, attention should also be paid to this matter to see whether the guilds are handling things in a practical manner."

Taxpayers' Association Asks the Municipal Council to Correct Illegal Electricity Charges; Letter from the Chinese and Western Merchandise Trade Market Reveals That the Electricity Company Charges are Not Based on Regulations 104

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Municipal Council yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, according to a letter from the Chinese and Western Merchandise Trade Market, 'Our market officially opened at the intersection of Zhian Temple Road and Xizang Road in this city on June 15th. All electricity was supplied by the Shanghai Electric Power Company starting on June 12th, and the market closed on July 14th. The electricity was used for a month and two days, totaling 5,949 kilowatt-hours. The number of kilowatt-hours on the bill sent by the company matches, but the electricity price is calculated at 1.2 silver yuan per kilowatt-hour. According to the company's electricity price list, the first 1,000 kilowatt-hours are charged at 1.2 silver yuan per kilowatt-hour, the next 1,000 kilowatt-hours are charged at 1 silver yuan per kilowatt-hour, the next 1,000 kilowatt-hours are charged at 6.5 *li* (0.0065 silver yuan) per kilowatt-hour, and the next 10,000 kilowatt-hours are charged at 5.5 *li* (0.0055 silver yuan) per kilowatt-hour. According to the above regulations, our market used a total of 5,949 kilowatt-hours, which should cost 501 taels and 1.1 silver yuan. However, the bill sent by the company is calculated at 1.2 silver yuan per kilowatt-hour, totaling 713 taels and 8.88 silver yuan, a difference of 211 taels and 6.8 silver yuan. We have sent a letter stating that we should correct the charges according to the electricity price regulations in order to resolve the matter. However, the company not only withheld the deposit paid by our market, but also replied on the 24th in a letter from the Deputy Secretary and Assistant General Accountant Mr. Hammon, stating, "I have received your letter of the 21st of this month regarding the temporary electricity bill for the New World building at No. 1 Jing'an Temple Road. I understand. After investigation, the bill is indeed calculated based on the price of this type of lighting. In this case, the company is unable to modify the bill. We are replying accordingly." The electricity price problem was still unresolved, so on the morning of the 26th, Mr. Dong Juesun, director of our market, personally went to the company to negotiate with the person in charge. However, the Chinese staff of the company did not know what regulations this calculation was based on, so they could not answer. Later, we went to the person in charge, a Westerner, who said that this electricity fee was calculated entirely according to Article 32 of the Shanghai Electric Power Company's Electricity Supply Rules. However, after checking the text of Article 32 of the rules, it concerns the method of electricity supply, but the calculation of electricity fees should still be based on the terms listed in the company's electricity price list. According to these regulations, the electricity fee should be charged according to the amount stipulated in the electricity price list, which is the correct method. However, the company relies on its monopoly power and disregards the regulations. Although we have repeatedly requested according to the regulations, it has refused to accept. Therefore, we have no choice but to attach a copy of the company's electricity price list and a copy of the company's electricity supply rules, and to inform you of the various situations in which our market has been illegally oppressed and forced to pay more for electricity. We implore your council to review the matter and immediately request that the Shanghai Electric Power Company, a public utility under your supervision, correct its illegal charges in accordance with the electricity price list and electricity supply rules, so as to prevent such illegal incidents from happening to the people of the city, and to resolve the dispute over the illegal mandatory surcharge on electricity fees for our market as soon as possible.' Article 32 of the Shanghai Electric Power Company's Electricity Supply Rules states, 'For temporary, short-term, or special electricity supply, this type of electricity supply can only be provided based on the terms listed in the price list and when the company has surplus power, transformers, generators, and other equipment that have not been sold.' Now that the time for supply has passed, the phrase 'and' to 'when' is not a problem. The problem is the price list on which it is based. If the Shanghai Electric Power Company only has one price list, which has been approved by your bureau, then even if this is short-term, it should be charged according to commercial lighting, which is undoubtedly legal. It is difficult to avoid miscalculations in calculating prices. The company does not correct the error even after the user has corrected it. It is obviously relying on the special privileges granted by taxpayers to seek illegal income or unjust enrichment. Based on the above, we hereby request that your bureau exercise the supervisory powers conferred by taxpayers in accordance with the law and immediately correct the above-mentioned errors of the Shanghai Electric Power Company to protect the legal interests of users. This is our earnest hope. Furthermore, the Shanghai Electric Company should use silver yuan as the standard for pricing. This is addressed to Mr. Fei, Acting Director of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession."

Japanese Trade Research Institute Invites Chinese Fishermen to Visit Fishing Grounds in Hokkaido 106

Dagong News: The Japanese Trade Research Institute in Shanghai has invited Chinese fishermen, including Yuan Kang and others, to visit fishing grounds in Hokkaido. The invited fishermen have already boarded the Nagasaki Maru to Japan. Details are as follows:

Purpose of the Invitation

Since the improvement of relations between China and Japan, the Japanese side has been using economic cooperation as a goal. The Japanese Ministry of Commerce and Industry has been using new trade policies to actively expand its strength in the Chinese market. It has decided to first engage in the improvement of commerce between China and Japan. It is trying to win back business by accommodating Chinese merchants who have significant trade relations with Japan, and it is expressing its feelings by restoring business. The purpose of this invitation by the Hokkaido Prefectural Trade Research Institute in Shanghai is to exchange and develop Japanese fishery products' trade with China, and to hold a so-called Sino-Japanese fishermen's friendship gathering.

Invited Fishermen

The Chinese fishermen invited to visit the fishing grounds in Hokkaido, Japan, include Ge Weian of Yuan Kang Company, Xiao Shenqing of Yu Chang Company, Chen Jinlin of Ding Yu Company, Wu Wengui of Yue Lai Company, Zheng Yunsheng of Sheng Ji Company, Liu Tonghua of Da Cheng Company, Weng Zhaofang of Gong Shun Company, and Zhang Houqing, and others, totaling over ten people. They will be accompanied by Fukushima Tadao, director of the Shanghai Trade Research Institute, and Yoshida Kyutaro, owner of the Yoshida Company, a Japanese fishing merchant in Shanghai. All hospitality will be very courteous.

Itinerary

The delegation of over ten people departed from Shanghai on the Nagasaki Maru on the 26th of last month. The itinerary is scheduled as follows: July 28th, arrival in Kobe; July 30th, Hakodate; August 1st, Otaru; August 3rd, Sapporo; August 8th, Baoshi; August 9th, Kushiro. They will visit various fishing ground facilities in the Hokkaido region, as well as factories for producing salted fish and cod (large-mouthed fish) products. It is scheduled to return to Shanghai in mid-August.

Three Robberies in a Row; Thieves Arrested Yesterday and Sent to Court 107

Shop Employees Describe What They Witnessed; All Three Thieves Give Evasive Testimony

The Great Prosperity Foreign Goods Store at 2063 Yangshupu Road, the Yuan Tai Chang Southern Goods Store at 2057 on the same road, and the Shanghai East Shoe and Hat Store at 15 Linqing Road were robbed of goods worth over 400 yuan by a large number of robbers at 8:30 PM the day before yesterday. The robbers fired warning shots when fleeing, and stray bullets injured a woman passing by. This has already been reported in this newspaper. Subsequently, Hua Detective Sun Afu, Detective Supervisor Su Yinggen, and Detective Wang Renzhong of the Yangshupu Police Station arrested three robbers, Zhao Baosheng, Xia Shoushan, and Gao Zikui, all from Funing, in the Lan Road and Hejian Road area. Fifteen yuan and two jiao were found on Zhao, seven yuan and two jiao on Xia, and nine yuan and seven jiao on Gao. All were taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer for the Municipal Council, stated the previous circumstances and requested a postponement. Following this, a report from the Chinese and Western detectives explained the circumstances of the arrest of the three defendants. A bullet found in the Great Prosperity Foreign Goods Store and the stolen money were presented to the court. Mi Xiangsheng, an employee of the Yuan Tai Chang Southern Goods Store, stated that three robbers entered at the time, two of whom had pistols, and identified the defendant Xia Shoushan as having robbed the store. Xiao Shousheng, an employee of the Great Prosperity Foreign Goods Store, stated that three robbers entered at the time, one of whom was outside the door acting as a lookout, and fired a shot when fleeing. The defendant Zhao Baosheng was present at the scene. Furthermore, an employee of the Zhang Maochang store stated that the appearance and clothing of the robber who was acting as a lookout outside the door were similar to those of the defendant Gao Zikui. At the time, a customer came to the store to buy goods, and the robber was watching him, preventing him from leaving. An apprentice in the store tried to move to the outside, and the robber fired a shot, but fortunately, it missed. Wu Dekun, an employee of the Linqing Road Shanghai East Shoe Store, stated that six robbers came at the time, all of whom had pistols, and identified the defendant Gao Zikui as being at the scene. When questioned, the three defendants gave evasive denials. Judge Xiao Xiefei ordered them to remain in custody for further investigation.

Includes Powerful Dum-Dum Bullets; Three Thieves with Illegal Intentions Arrested

Hua Detective Shang Wu and Detective Supervisor Wang Youshan of the Huishi Police Station learned at around 7:00 AM on the 31st of last month that a gang of thieves was gathering at the intersection of Xiamen Road and Zhejiang Road, plotting illegal activities. They immediately went to the location with Western detectives and arrested three thieves, Li Caigen, from Tongzhou, Xia Jinsheng, a local, and Du Atong (also known as Tong ?, from Pudong). Two pistols and thirteen bullets, including five Dum-Dum bullets, were found in a shoebox behind Li's No. 16948 bicycle. The bullets are very powerful, exploding upon firing. All were taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer for the Municipal Council, stated the previous circumstances and charged the three defendants with violating Article 1 of the Regulations for the Prohibition of Military Firearms and Weapons, and stated that the defendants said at the police station that the guns and bullets belonged to Yan Changgen, who lived at 1639, Lane 586, Yinxiang Port. Detectives went to arrest him but could not find him. The case is still under investigation, so he requested permission to extend the hearing. Chen Mengyu Sentenced for Swindling His Uncle 110

Sentenced to Three Years Imprisonment

Chen Zhilian, owner of the Hua Feng Soap Factory from Shaoxing, had been receiving threatening letters demanding large sums of money. Chen reported this to the General Police Station, and after investigation by Hua Detectives Su Changsheng and Li Yilian and Detective Supervisor Li Jincheng, it was learned that the case was the work of Chen's nephew Chen Mengyu (also known as Mengyu or Yuansheng), owner of the Jinlang Cosmetics Company. He was arrested, along with his accomplices Song Nianhong, the woman Zhu Wangshi, and the suspect Wu Depei (Chen Zhilian's nephew), and sent to the First Special Court for trial. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Qian Hongye of the Criminal Court continued the trial in Criminal Court One. After lawyer Jiang Baolian of the police station stated everything, he further charged Chen Mengyu with the crime of manufacturing explosives under Article 187 of the Criminal Law. The court then questioned the defendants. Finding the facts clear, the judge ordered the debate to begin. After lawyers Jiang of the police station and Fan Gang, lawyer of the defendant, debated, Judge Qian immediately announced the verdict in court. Chen Mengyu was sentenced to three years' imprisonment for attempted extortion, but was found not guilty of the charge of manufacturing explosives. Song Nianhong and Zhu Wangshi were each sentenced to three months' imprisonment, suspended for three years. Wu Depei was found not guilty. Song and Zhu were each released on bail pending appeal.

Kidnappers from Suqian Arrested in Pudong 114

French Concession Police Raid Rickshaws Yesterday 115

Rickshaw Company Representatives Petitioned the City Government, Rickshaw Pullers Held a Meeting Yesterday Vowing Strong Opposition

According to sources in the rickshaw business, since the French Concession announced rickshaw registration, a month has passed. Rickshaw pullers are dissatisfied with the registration process, and the registration fees are too burdensome. They unanimously refused to register. The French authorities took coercive measures and decisively acted, dispatching a large number of detectives starting at 9:00 AM yesterday morning to seize rickshaws and order pullers to register. The pullers abandoned their rickshaws and refused to register. The police stations were filled with impounded rickshaws, totaling seven to eight hundred. Having lost their livelihoods after their rickshaws were seized, the pullers, leading the old and young, requested assistance from the Rickshaw Trade Association and various charities along the way.

Rickshaw Company Meeting

Regarding the French Concession seizing rickshaws, rickshaw owners held a large meeting at 9:00 AM yesterday on Sanguantang Road to discuss countermeasures. Over three hundred owners attended. Resolutions were passed: (1) To sympathize with the pullers' demands to protect their business, a united action will be taken. (2) The obligation of rickshaws in business is to pay taxes. Rickshaw puller registration is a separate issue. Vehicle taxes have not been reduced, yet the French Concession is preventing rickshaws from operating because of the puller registration problem. The French Municipal Council should bear the responsibility for the resulting damages and disputes. (3) To oppose the French Concession's high-handed measures. (4) Representatives Qiu Chunshan, Zhang Huaiyang, and Yu Dajin were elected to petition the city government.

Representatives' Petition

The rickshaw company representatives Qiu Chunshan, Zhang Huaiyang, Yu Dajin, etc., took a petition to the Municipal Government's Bureau of Social Affairs at 2:00 PM yesterday. Representatives were sent to meet them. The representatives stated the rickshaw companies' difficulties and requested the government to consider the pullers' livelihoods and protect the rickshaw companies' business. The Bureau of Social Affairs representatives agreed to forward their concerns to the French authorities for consideration. The representatives left satisfied.

Petition

The petition is excerpted below: Submitted regarding the French Concession Police Department forcing rickshaw puller registration, impounding rickshaws, and prohibiting operation, leaving pullers unable to settle down, and the situation is tense, requesting negotiations to stop this to prevent accidents. The French Concession Police Department announced that since the public rickshaw puller registration began last month, the association believes the pullers are ignorant and, upon hearing the news, unanimously expressed that they would rather beg than register. After repeated requests, the association asked them to stop this but the French authorities ignored public opinion and did not change the method. They intensified their actions against the 1,100 French-licensed rickshaws (numbers 16001 to 17100) that were not registered last month. From today, the police will impound them one by one and force the pullers and owners to register at the police station, with 700 to 800 rickshaws being seized. More than 1,000 pullers suddenly became unemployed, and public sentiment reached a boiling point. They came to the association requesting relief. The association has repeatedly and earnestly advised them to wait for a solution, but the situation is urgent, and social order is greatly affected. Therefore, we specially recommend representatives Qiu Chunshan, Zhang Huaiyang, and Yu Dajin to petition Your Excellency (Bureau) to immediately negotiate with the French Concession authorities to stop this and prevent accidents to maintain social order, in anticipation of your urgent orders.

Rickshaw Pullers' Meeting Following the rickshaw seizures by the French police, the number of unemployed has increased dramatically, and the situation is extremely serious. A mass meeting was held at 1:00 PM yesterday at the South Wharf. Shi Changsheng was elected chairman. Resolutions were passed: (1) To unanimously oppose registration. (2) To elect representatives to request assistance from party and government organizations and the rickshaw trade association. (3) In secret. It is also heard that the rickshaw pullers' representatives will hold a large petition at the Municipal Government's Bureau of Social Affairs and relevant parties today.

News from the French Police Station. The French Concession authorities, because rickshaw owners are organized to obstruct rickshaw puller registration, implemented the measures published in the newspapers on the 26th of last month, seizing 215 rickshaws that should have been registered in July. Because French police officers used peaceful means, no accidents occurred. After questioning by police officers at the police station, some pullers said they did not receive orders from their owners, so they did not register, or said they did not know registration had started. Some said their owners did not allow them to register. The Chinese and foreign newspapers have recently published many reports on this issue, but they are not entirely accurate. They are presented separately as follows: (1) The French Concession authorities have no intention of restricting the number of rickshaws and have explained to rickshaw owners that all pullers will be registered, regardless of the number of pullers. (2) The French Concession authorities have proven through various sources that the rickshaw pullers' resistance to registration and various incitements and rumors are caused by rickshaw owners, and not the pullers' own intention. Rickshaw owners are simply misunderstanding that once rickshaw pullers are registered, their power to inspect the pullers will be deprived. However, yesterday, many rickshaw pullers voluntarily registered according to the regulations set by the French Concession authorities.

Zhu Baoxian Goes to England to Study 116

The famous lawyer Mr. Zhu Shixian, the second son of the industrial magnate Mr. Zhu Gengtao, graduated from Shanghai Chizhi University with a Bachelor of Arts degree. In the same year, he was awarded a Bachelor of Laws degree from Soochow Law School and was elected as a member of the Phi Tau Phi Scholastic Honor Society. He served as a specialist member of the Constitution Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan of the National Government, making many contributions to the draft constitution. After the constitution was completed, he came to Shanghai to practice law, protecting human rights, and was praised by all parties. Recently, he was sent to England by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees to study law for three years. Mr. Zhu aims to promote the culture of the motherland while appropriately adopting the strengths of other countries' cultures. During his study abroad, he will concentrate on this. Upon his return to the country after completing his studies, his contributions will not be limited to law alone. Mr. Zhu's recently authored "English Translation and Annotation of Chinese Civil Law" will be published by Shanghai Zengwentang soon. The content is rich, and the arguments are correct, making it a rare English legal book. Mr. Zhu is scheduled to travel to England on the (Kaisar—I—Hino) on August 6. Friends and relatives have been hosting farewell parties, keeping him very busy.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed Requesting Prohibition of Inland Business of the International Savings Society 118

Violates the Original Intention of National Legislation Restricting It

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, saying: "To the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: As a result of the implementation of our country's new criminal law on July 1, the International Savings Society has closed its inland branches in non-treaty ports. Depositors everywhere are very anxious about their previous deposits and have repeatedly sent letters to the association to inquire about news. The association forwarded inquiries to the International Savings Society, which replied that it hopes depositors will deposit their due deposits at local branches. Although the inland branches have been closed, the inland deposits have not been ended, and the collection has not been stopped. Depositors must send their deposits monthly to their branches, which are relatively far apart, resulting in more trouble and expense. It has been found that foreign merchants operating inland business has always been strictly prohibited by treaties. Now, by closing branches, the name of inland business is cleverly avoided, but the deposits have not been ended, and the reality of inland business is still maintained, which is not permitted by the treaty. For the sake of depositors and the treaty, Your Ministry should have a way to properly handle this situation; otherwise, it will only cause suffering to the inland depositors, and it will not help the original intention of national legislation restricting it. Should negotiations be held with the French side to order the end of the collection of inland deposits and the return of the deposits? We await instructions for compliance. Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce."

Conclusion of Trial of Two Women Arguing Over Child 122

Will Be Pronounced on the 5th of This Month Who Will Ultimately Have Custody Is Unknown

Chen Zhou, the wife of the late real estate tycoon and Catholic Chen Yide, residing at No. 260 Belle Road, French Concession, was sued in the Civil Court of the Second Special District Court by Chen Yipei, his husband's mistress residing at No. 2 Jiusili, Pushi Road, through lawyer, to return her biological son, Xiong Guan (also known as Nengyi). After repeated hearings by Judge Ma Yishu of the court, because the testimonies of both parties insisted that the child was their own biological child, it was decided that both parties should bring the child and send them to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for scientific identification. The result was that both defendants had the possibility of giving birth to Chen Xiong Guan, and it was proven that the defendant Chen Zhou had indeed been pregnant and given birth before. After replying to the court, the plaintiff requested an investigation into the Ten Thousand Years Book at the Catholic Church to prove whether Chen Zhou had given birth to children, since Chen Yide was a Catholic and should have registered his children in accordance with church regulations. This matter has been reported in the newspapers many times. This case was again heard by Judge Ma of the Second Special District Court yesterday. The plaintiff Chen Yipei and her lawyer were present in court. The defendant Chen Zhou was represented by a lawyer. The court announced that after the court had investigated the Catholic Church, the reply stated that Chen Yide was not a member of the church, and there was no way to investigate the child's registration. The plaintiffs' representatives, Zhang Ding, Ma Nangeng, and Peng Qixiu, stood up one after another and stated that during the trial, obstetrician He Cuizhen had testified, proving that the plaintiff had given birth and that she had delivered the baby. Photos of the plaintiff and Chen Yide when they lived together and with Xiong Guan were presented. The appraisal report of the Forensic Institute is vague on all points of the appraisal, saying that both parties can produce Chen Xiong Guan, and the result has no basis and can be ignored. As for the appearance and skeletal structure, although it is recognized in science that there is no accurate identification by Jiaoxue Qian, it can be found that the First Special District Court has a case in which Zhang Zhuying and Zhou confirmed their biological son. The institute identified the appearance and anatomical position as essential elements of heredity, which is obviously unfair and difficult to convince. It is requested that another expert be selected for re-identification, and that the defendant be ordered to bring Xiong Guan to the court for comparison with the plaintiff in court, so that the court can freely determine who to believe. Judge Ma ruled that the Forensic Institute is sponsored by the Ministry of Justice and Administration, and there is no need for further inspection. Chen Xiong Guan's photos have also been presented, and there is no need to summon him to court. At this point, the court considered the investigation of evidence to be complete, the facts to be clear, and then ordered the start of the debate. The lawyers of both sides debated each other, and the arguments were quite fierce. It took an hour before they stopped. The court declared the debate over and scheduled the pronouncement for 10:00 AM on the 5th of this month, and then adjourned.

Preserving the Local Area and Bankrolling Was Approved by Jiangsu Province

Xu Mao, Lin Kanghou, and Shen Yongshi, representatives of public organizations in Shanghai, presented to Cai Kong regarding Wang Binyan, head of the Zhabei Defense Corps, preserving the local area and bankrolling, and the contract establishing State Manufacturing Bureau property as collateral, because Wang's bankruptcy has been forced. The original text reads: (Omitted above) The investigation found that in October of the 13th year of the Republic of China, on the night the Jiangsu-Zhejiang war ended, more than 40,000 troops and more than 10,000 refugees suddenly came to Zhabei. People were panicked, and order was chaotic. Wang Binyan, head of the Zhabei Defense Corps, repeatedly received telegrams from Han Guojun, the former governor of Jiangsu Province and the director of military rehabilitation, ordering him to maintain the local area, provide rations for the troops, and raise funds for cooking, which was approved as a regular expenditure item. At that time, local officials had fled, and the police wages had not been paid. The Chamber of Commerce had not yet been established, and all factories had stopped work. In the name of the Zhabei Charity Corps, he appealed for loans, which were all handled by Wang Binyan, with great results. The local area was spared from ruin, and the people were spared from disaster. The total amount of bankrolled silver dollars was 228,649.70, which was registered and reported for approval. Subsequently, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance was sent to Shanghai to sign a contract and inform the Ministry of the Army for the record, with all the land of the State-owned Shanghai Manufacturing Bureau as collateral. To date, no money has been returned. However, in this bankrolled amount, Wang Binyan mortgaged his personal residence property deed to Guangdong Bank, Hong Kong National Bank, and Cunde Qianzhuang for 10,000 taels of silver each. To date, more than ten years have passed, and calculated at one principal and one interest, he owes a total of 60,000 taels of silver, equivalent to 84,000 yuan. It has been mortgaged repeatedly, and now the three villages have been terminated. Unless the money is returned in full, the property will be seized and sold and he will be unable to live there. The businesses were located in Zhabei and handled this matter together. The eyes of Wang Binyan are sharp. He was forced to act in the public interest, preserving the local area. He has served as the director of the Zhabei Charity Corps and the head of the Defense Corps throughout his life. He has been honest and has no savings. Under the pressure of this predicament, he is facing the worry of his entire family going bankrupt. According to public opinion, they are all willing to appeal for him. It has been explained to Shanghai Local Association President Du Yuesheng, who also said that as a public duty for all of Shanghai, there are many who have taken on local responsibilities, and it is too unjust to allow Wang Binyan to be in such a difficult situation without help. In addition to asking President Du to personally ask the minister for relief, this public presentation has been prepared, with a photographic contract attached, requesting Your Ministry to consider that the Shanghai Manufacturing Bureau is state-owned property, which has already been mortgaged on record. Could you please approve the prior return of a portion, which Wang Binyan will claim, and the rest will be settled later when the finances are more prosperous. The merchants are speaking out righteously to prove for Wang Binyan that it was indeed his private property that was hastily mortgaged and transferred for local public use. There is a contract with the seal and signature of Han Guojun, the former governor of Jiangsu Province and the director of military rehabilitation, and there is also a contract stating that the Ministry of the Army was informed for the record, with no fabrication. We hereby declare and present this to Minister of Finance Kong, with a photographic contract attached. Murderer Tao Yongchang Continues to Cause Trouble in Prison; One Wave Subsides, Another Rises; Demands Transfer and Insults Warden 133

Murderer Tao Yongchang, nicknamed Xiao Xizi, along with accomplices Xiao Taizhou and Wang Wangjiao Ahu, shot and killed Cao Adi, a Jiangyin dockyard ruffian, at a small general assembly hall on Minguo Road outside the Xiaodongmen in the French Concession at the end of June 1933. After the incident, Tao immediately went into hiding, and the French police issued an arrest warrant but were unable to apprehend him. In the summer of last year, Tao was passing by Tangshan Road in Hongkou when he was spotted by the wife of the deceased, Cao Adi, who raised the alarm and had him arrested and handed over to the Public Concession police, who transferred him to the French police and the Special District Court for prosecution. The trial concluded with a fifteen-year prison sentence. The convicted criminal refused to accept the ruling and appealed to the Third Branch of the Higher Court, which upheld the original verdict. The criminal still refused to accept the decision and appealed to the Supreme Court for a first instance appeal. During the appeal period, the criminal was held in the detention center of the Special District Court. However, in June of this year, the criminal dared to collude with fellow inmates Wang Deyu and Wang Yuhe, who were also murderers, to extort money from Wang Xinggao, the mastermind behind another murder case, who had been sentenced to life imprisonment and was currently appealing. Wang Xinggao sent a letter to the French Police Department reporting the extortion. The French police took Tao Yongchang, Wang Deyu, Wang Yuhe, and the informant Wang Xinggao into custody for investigation and handed them over to the Special District Court for prosecution. Judge Zhang Chaozuo concluded the investigation, sentencing Tao Yongchang to six months in prison. Wang Deyu and Wang Yuhe were found not guilty. Tao still refused to accept the verdict and is currently appealing to the Third Branch of the Higher Court. The Supreme Court has already announced its judgment on the criminal's murder case, reducing his sentence by one year. Once the judgment and case files are sent to the Third Branch of the Higher Court, he will be transferred to prison to serve his sentence. However, the criminal has been quite restless in the detention center. Last month, he participated with other inmates in a ritual of worshipping Li Guocheng as the "old man," throwing away slop buckets and causing a disturbance by hitting people. After being taken for investigation by the French police, he was sent back and placed in heavy shackles. Unexpectedly, the criminal recently stirred up trouble again. Because of the hot weather recently, Tao was held in the West Wing, where the air was not circulating and was very stuffy. He requested that the warden of the detention center transfer him to the East Wing, which is attached to the Special Prison on Masnan Road, because it was more spacious than the West Wing. The warden refused his request, and Tao harbored resentment but did not express it verbally. Instead, he wrote insulting notes inside the prison, calling the warden and other officials "lackeys." The detention center discovered the notes and reported them to the warden, who questioned Tao. Tao not only refused to submit but also used abusive language and was defiant. The warden ordered Tao to be transferred to the French police for investigation and prosecution. The day before yesterday, the police sent Tao to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Special District Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo questioned him. A lawyer from the Police Department, Chen, explained the case and prosecuted him for insulting public officials. Judge Zhang was furious at the offender's audacity in acting lawlessly within a place of law and stated that he deserved no mercy. According to Tao's confession, the notes were written by a Mr. Zhang, a former opium addict who had just been released from prison. He claimed that he had been well-behaved in prison before, but he was now demanding improved treatment because the current conditions in prison were too harsh. The court reviewed the confession and ordered further investigation and interrogation. The defendant was remanded to custody.

Old Woman Beats Husband's Brother to Death; Yang Goushi Flees and is Arrested 134

Yang Xunshi, a woman from Baoying, Jiangbei, is sixty-three years old. She originally farmed for a living in her hometown and had two sons. Because her husband's older brother, Yang Shunkang, had no children, she gave him her eldest son as an heir. In 1930, Yang had disagreements with Shunkang, and over time, their animosity deepened. She then plotted to harm him but had no opportunity. On June 8th of that year, while Shunkang was working in the fields, Yang led several people, grabbed Shunkang, beat him severely, and pushed him into the river, where he drowned. His family managed to retrieve his body and place it in a coffin. Yang fled without a trace. Subsequently, her clan reported the incident to the county, and an autopsy confirmed that he had been murdered. An arrest warrant was issued for Yang. Ding Ziwen, the local bailiff of the county, came to Shanghai with Xun Guizhen, a member of the clan, and discovered that Yang Goushi was hiding in a straw shed at the lime kiln in Xiaoshadu, West Shanghai. The day before yesterday afternoon, they went to the Caojiadu Public Security Sub-bureau, which dispatched police to the address and arrested Yang, taking her back to the bureau. After an interrogation by Officer Liu, she was transferred to the main bureau for further investigation due to the case involving the murder of her husband's brother.

Boat Owner Wang Yifa Drowns 135

Yesterday morning around 7 AM, Wang Yifa, a 25-year-old ferry owner from No. 15 Dongjiadu, was operating a ferry carrying passengers from east to west. Just a few zhang away from the dock, Wang, standing at the bow of the boat, lost his footing and fell into the river while using a pole to propel the boat. He immediately drowned. Efforts to recover his body were unsuccessful. It wasn't until noon that Wang's body was found near the dock. His family took the body home. The police station in charge of the area was informed and instructed the local bailiff to report the incident to the court for an autopsy.

Ten-Year-Old Female Student Tragically Killed by Car 136

Huang Hanting, from Jiujiang, works at a foreign firm and lives at No. 29 Cihou Lane, Hartung Road. His daughter, Huang Cuizhen, is ten years old, exceptionally intelligent, and studies at Nanli Industrial Elementary School, consistently ranking at the top of her class, earning the love of her teachers. On the morning of the 30th of last month, around 6 AM, she was going to school. Because the lesson time had not arrived, she went to a classmate's home on Fuxu Road to the south. As she was about to reach the sidewalk, she was suddenly struck by a self-owned car No. 6474, driven by Qiu Feihai, which was traveling west. It is unknown how, but he mistakenly drove south, knocking Cuizhen down and seriously injuring her. He did not rush her to the hospital for treatment. By the time the police medical car arrived and transported Cuizhen to the hospital for treatment, she had lost too much blood and died without receiving adequate medical care. The prosecutor dispatched by the First Special District Court conducted an autopsy, confirming that she had died from the injuries sustained in the collision. Huang Hanting has retained lawyers Fan Gang and Huang Xuanzhang to file a criminal lawsuit to seek legal protection.

Grand Opening of Children's Year in the Capital: Child Representatives Pay Respects at the Mausoleum and Present Flowers, Ceremony Held with Important Figures Offering Encouragement 150

Then, Gu delivered an opening speech explaining the meaning of Children's Year, stating that, "From now on, we want to launch a broad and universal movement to promote the happiness and education of children throughout the country. At the same time, we must give great importance to this cause. We should adopt a ten-year determination for national restoration through production and education, and carry it out effectively to achieve the goal of national revival." Kong Xiangxi Gives Four Instructions

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 1st) At the opening ceremony of Children's Year in the capital, Kong Xiangxi delivered a speech, the gist of which is as follows: "The meaning and purpose of Children's Year is to cultivate healthy citizens and save the country from its precarious situation. However, the foundation of the nation is children, so education is the most important thing for children, and training is the second. Whether children are of school age or not, they should be effectively educated by schools or families, and children should be trained with the inherent virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace of our nation. I would like to put forward a few points that should be noted in all aspects of Children's Year for reference: (1) The Party and government should formulate laws and regulations to protect children, support appropriate child welfare organizations, and prohibit the abuse of children in society; (2) Society should be enthusiastic about child welfare undertakings and organize activities that are beneficial to children as much as possible; (3) Families should fully understand how to strengthen children's physique and increase their knowledge, so as to fulfill their parents' responsibility of education; (4) Children should know how to endure hardship, be self-reliant, and strive to be good citizens. In the family, they should start by being filial and fraternal, and only in this way can they shoulder great responsibilities for the country in the future. The above four points are just an outline. I hope everyone can implement them practically, so that the foundation of the country can be consolidated, the nation can be revived, and we will not fail the meaning of today's meeting."

Little Men (2) 151

— Originally written by Ms. Alcott of the United States, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

The house seemed to be filled with children, who were spending the misty, drizzly evening in various forms of entertainment. Clearly, the children filled every corner—"upstairs, downstairs, and in the landlady's room"—because through several open doors one could see happy groups of big children, little children, and children of all sizes, all engaged in various pastimes. Although the styles differed, the result was very noisy. Two large rooms on the right were clearly classrooms, because here only desks, maps, blackboards, and scattered books were visible. A roaring fire burned in the stove, and several lazy boys were reclining near the stove by the wall, discussing a new ball game, so excited that only their boots could be seen flailing in the air. A tall youth was practicing playing the flute at his leisure, undisturbed by the noise around him. Two or three others were straddling desks, pausing occasionally to catch their breath, and one small comedian was making humorous cartoons of all their companions, eliciting much laughter and joy.

In a room on the left, a long dining table was set up, with several large bottles of fresh milk, piles of yellow and white bread, and dazzling gingerbread neatly stacked on top. How precious these were in the hearts of the children! Suddenly, the aroma of baked bread wafted through the air, mixed with the scent of baked apples. How could these not tempt a hungry little tummy and little nose?

However, the scene that impressed him the most was in the small opening inside the door, that is, in the stairwell. At the very top, a lively tug-of-war was in progress. The top platform of one section was being used for a game of jacks, another for a chessboard, and on each of the steps, a boy was reading a book, a girl was singing a lullaby to her doll, two puppies, a kitten, and a string of little boys were sliding down the handrail, regardless of the fact that this was very detrimental to their clothes and could easily endanger their limbs.

Over a Thousand Children from Our City Participated in Yesterday's Children's Year Opening Ceremony 152
