Child representatives Chen Zhuting from Xicheng, Chen Zhitong from Commercial Press, and Shen Jichuan from the Health Camp then gave responses. The Children's Year song was sung before the event concluded.

Mayor's Speech

Mayor Wu said in his opening speech: "Members of the presidium, ladies and gentlemen, children, today is the opening of the nationally designated Children's Year. It is a great honor for the citizens of Shanghai to celebrate the opening of Children's Year here, because Children's Year was proposed by the city of Shanghai and approved by the National Government. From today until July 31st next year, administrative agencies and public organizations across the country will strive to promote and implement children's affairs during this year. Children are the seeds of the Chinese nation, and they are the continuation of the life of the Chinese nation. The rise and fall of the future of the Chinese nation depends entirely on whether today's Chinese children have hope. Whether today's children have hope depends on the responsibility of today's parents, today's society, and the government. The government, society, and parents must bear the responsibility of educating children. Therefore, the National Government has designated this year as Children's Year to instill the concept of caring for children in the people of the whole country, and at the same time to make children aware of the importance of their own position. China has too shallow a concept of the nation, and too deep a concept of the family. If we can transfer the concept of planning for the family to planning for the nation, I believe the Chinese nation would not have today's situation. Even if we have today's situation, we can break through this difficulty. Unfortunately, the people of the whole country still only plan for their families and clans, and not for the entire nation. Therefore, although there are 450 million people, accounting for a quarter of the world's population, they are still oppressed, bullied, and dominated by a small number of ethnic groups. The reason for this is that the 450 million people are like a plate of loose sand, with no unity, only planning for individuals and families, and not for the entire nation. This is the first reason. The first reason is that we only know how to pass on the seeds, but we don't know how to cultivate the seeds. What is the use of having many people if they are not educated? Instead, they are oppressed, bullied, and dominated by ethnic groups with fewer people but more education. Because we only know how to pass on the seeds and don't know how to cultivate them, so more people cannot generate more strength. Han Feizi said, 'Millions of ignorant people are called no people.' This is the principle. The ancient saying goes, 'There are three unfilial acts, and having no descendants is the greatest.' If we only pass on descendants for a family, but do not educate them, they will become prodigal sons. If we pass on descendants for a nation, but they have no knowledge, they will become a nation-destroying seed. Therefore, from now on, the government, society, and parents must bear the responsibility of educating children, so that they can not only prosper a family, but also revive the nation. Otherwise, not taking responsibility for education will result in prodigal sons and nation-destroying seeds. Therefore, during this nationally designated Children's Year, we must not only strive to promote and implement children's affairs, but also awaken the attention of the people of the whole country to have a new concept of children, and awaken the attention of children across the country to recognize that today's children are the future masters of China, and they are the ones who will continue the life of the Chinese nation. We must value our position ourselves. Therefore, it is meaningful for representatives of children from all over the city to celebrate the opening of Children's Year here today. The Municipal Government will strive to promote children's affairs within its capabilities, especially children's affairs for the poor. The Municipal Government has planned to build 3,000 houses for the poor. In the new villages for the poor, there will be simple clinics, elementary schools, children's parks, and children's nurseries, so that poor children can receive appropriate education. However, children's affairs are great, and cannot be done by the government alone. I hope people from all walks of life will work together to promote them."

Cai's Speech

Cai Hongtian, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, said in his speech, "Today is the first day of the nationally designated Children's Year. Children are the foundation of the nation, and we must pay special attention to the education and protection of children. Therefore, the government has designated 24 years as the nationally designated Children's Year. Today's opening ceremony is to start promoting children's affairs from today. Children are the future masters of the country. We must cultivate children with the spirit of craftsmen, so that they can protect the country in the future, just like craftsmen protect houses and gardens. But to cultivate their spirit of craftsmen, they must forge a healthy physique and instill rich knowledge."

Children's Responses

(1) Chen Zhuting from Xicheng Elementary School said, "Children, today is the opening day of Children's Year, and it is the most memorable day. The mayor and officials from various agencies have spent a lot of effort and financial resources to make today's ceremony possible. How should we be grateful? We children are the center of human society, and we must love society, the country, and even humanity, and take responsibility for serving society and the country. I hope for the care of people in society, and I hope we will work hard ourselves." (2) Chen Zhitong, a child laborer from the Commercial Press, said, "Ladies and gentlemen, it is a great honor to be here today to contribute my opinions as a child representative. The government's designation of Children's Year and the holding of today's grand ceremony are of great significance. It is entirely to improve our environment and raise our living standards. Today's children will be tomorrow's adults. Disregarding today's children is disregarding tomorrow's adults. If a country wants to be strong, it must have strong children to produce strong adults to take on major responsibilities. Today, we children thank the government for its attention, and at the same time, we must study hard, exercise our bodies, use domestic products, and implement the New Life Movement." (3) Shen Jichuan from the Children's Summer Health Camp said, "Ladies and gentlemen, students, in the current era, no one can deny that today's children are the future masters of the country, but we must study hard and exercise our bodies, so that we can shoulder the responsibility of being masters in the future. I hope everyone will work hard, the strength or weakness of the country in the future depends entirely on us."

The Dispute Over Co-educational Schools in Private Middle Schools in Beiping Has Not Ended 154

Representatives of the Private Middle School Federation Firmly Demand the Original Telegram of Instructions from the Ministry of Education

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The issue of co-educational schools in Beiping is getting bigger and bigger. The Municipal Government insists on not allowing co-education and ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to strictly ban co-educational schools in all private middle schools. The Private Middle School Federation submitted a petition to the Ministry of Education, requesting the Ministry to stop the Beiping authorities from banning co-educational schools, so as not to conflict with the middle school regulations. The Private Middle School Federation held a secret meeting in Zhongshan Park today to discuss further measures, but before the facts are successful, the deliberation resolutions must be kept absolutely confidential. The attitude of the Ministry of Education is particularly noteworthy. At present, Qiuzhongfang hopes that the Ministry of Education will give some instructions so as to resolve the dispute as soon as possible. The Municipal Government has always insisted on the "banning of co-educational schools", so it is not easy to resolve the dispute for a while. The situation of all parties is recorded as follows:

Attitude of the Ministry of Education

One week after the Beiping co-educational school dispute occurred, the Ministry of Education sent a telegram to the Beiping Education Authorities, giving some instructions. The Social Affairs Bureau did not publicize the original telegram due to certain reasons, and only stated that the Ministry of Education had approved the issue of gender-separated schools in principle. Representatives of private middle schools said that the Ministry of Education did not approve the Beiping authorities' proposal. The Private Middle School Federation had previously telegraphed the Ministry of Education, requesting that the original plan for co-educational schools be maintained. The Ministry of Education has now issued an approval to Beiping. The original text is as follows: "I have received the report. I have given detailed instructions on the plan submitted to the Ministry by the Social Affairs Bureau. Please wait for the Bureau to comply." Regarding the two points of the original telegram of the Ministry of Education, "detailed instructions" and "wait for the Bureau to comply", the Private Middle School Federation expressed doubts, so it is necessary to read the original telegram of the Ministry of Education to the Social Affairs Bureau. However, as of press time, the Social Affairs Bureau has not allowed access to the telegram, and the truth is still unknown.

Private Middle School Representatives Speak

According to representatives of private middle schools, the Beiping Social Affairs Bureau, based on the instructions of the Municipal Government, banned co-educational schools and founded the Second Municipal Girls' Middle School, enrolling students in the second grade and above, which is an illegal act. Article 23 of the Ministry of Education's Middle School Regulations states that "newly established middle schools shall not enroll students in the third grade or above in the first year, and shall not enroll students in the third grade or above in the second year." Therefore, the newly established Beiping Municipal Second Girls' Middle School violated the Ministry of Education's Middle School Regulations by enrolling female students from the second and third grades of various private middle schools in the first year. Co-educational schools are consistent across the country, why is Beiping unique? Private middle schools in Beiping have vocational commercial or normal courses, but the Municipal Girls' Middle School does not have such courses, only ordinary classes. Now the Beiping authorities are forcing female students from private middle schools to transfer to the Municipal Girls' Middle School. How can they be accommodated? In short, even if the Social Affairs Bureau violates the intentions of the Ministry of Education, private middle schools will still enroll female students and maintain Beiping's inherent educational achievements before the Ministry of Education has expressly abolished the middle school regulations.

Circular from the Social Affairs Bureau

It has been found that this city has strictly implemented gender-separated schools in middle schools and has ordered all private boys' middle schools (note: the authorities call them boys' middle schools, but private middle schools only call themselves a certain private middle school, such as Northern Middle School, North China Middle School, Wenzhi Middle School, etc., and no school is specifically called a boys' middle school) not to enroll female students, and ordered all co-educational private middle schools to report the female students in the second and third grades, and the female students of each school may apply to this bureau for registration, so as to find ways to accommodate them. Now it is found that some schools still publish advertisements for enrollment that also accept female students. I am afraid that female students who should go to school do not understand the truth and still go to apply. This is a further announcement that the student status of female students who are admitted to various private boys' middle schools will not be approved by this bureau. In addition to strictly ordering each private middle school to stop this practice, it is appropriate to announce it to the public, and each should pay attention to it and apply to the Municipal Private Girls' Middle School to avoid harming themselves. This is a special announcement.

Snippets 163

A clay statue of a god or a wooden Buddha statue can suppress countless people and reactionary forces with more power than hundreds of thousands of troops.

Studying is like sailing. You cannot reach your destination without experiencing the twists and turns of dangerous winds and waves.

When poor, one will sympathize with the poor and hate the rich; when rich, one will sympathize with the rich and hate the poor. People are like this, and I am like this, but I don't feel it at the moment.

Those who speak ill of others in front of you will also speak ill of you in front of others.

The tortoise wins the tortoise-hare race, which shows that the wise are often not as good as the foolish. The same is true for writers who have become famous and those who have not.

When studying, speculating on worldly affairs seems to be enough to deal with, but if you step into society one day, you will feel at a loss and pain will arise, so you will be timid and unwilling to move forward, or even go astray. Therefore, the disease of arrogance must be guarded against at school.

Summer at Xuanwu Lake 164

— Su Qin

In the summer, going to Xuanwu Lake will make people mistakenly believe that it is early autumn. Everywhere is a lush green, everywhere is a dense layer of shade, the scenery is always so quiet, and the ends of the four houses are silent without any sound.

But, do you say it is too depressed and too deserted? But it is not. Look, on the lake over there, aren't there many children and women rowing boats? On the tea seats over there, aren't there dozens or hundreds of people? However, you can't hear any noise.

Relying on the city root of Fengrun Gate, there is full of clear lake water. Unknown aquatic plants, when you paddle past, are sandwiched between newly born lotus leaves and newly blooming lotus flowers, floating on the water, shaking slightly. You must appreciate that kind of rough-line charm.

Otherwise, you pick a sunny afternoon, if you are not afraid of the sun, run to the upper floor of Jiming Temple, or simply walk to Taicheng, and you will have a leisurely look at Xuanwu Lake. You see that distant Jiangshan Mountain, the undulating ridges and peaks, a purple-golden peak shadow, as if it is rushing straight into the heart of the lake. Go and imagine that kind of majestic and beautiful scenery.

At that time, that heroic and unrestrained mood is unique to you, even though the sun makes you sweat all over. This look can be done in spring or autumn, but in spring, the reflections in the lake do not have heavy colors, and in autumn, the lake is too desolate. Only in summer, there is such fun.

As for the lake scenery under the moonlit night, I don't want to talk about it. If you have the experience of "lake tour on a moonlit night", you can always know something. Let's just say, it has a different interest compared to the night market in Confucius Temple and on the Qinhuai River. It might be better under the starlight. Because the night scene is hazy, the shallow lake around it will make you feel like it is a vast ocean, and the future is so dark and dark, all of it.

Aviation Romance 165

— Yan Yun

Modern science is prosperous, and the precision of machines is not only ingenious, but also can promote human marriage. As I have heard, it is a good story. A certain female student of a certain university in the ancient capital, born with beauty, has a famous reputation for a while. The pursuers of the opposite sex are all from Gansu Province, and they respect her as the Queen of the Frontier. Gu Hou's seat is abundant and her nature is high and arrogant, despising the masses and seldom allowing it. One day, she received an electric report saying that her mother was seriously ill and urged her to return immediately. The woman thought that she was separated by thousands of miles and it was difficult to fly. So she sought a plan from the China Travel Service. The people in the company told her that Eurasia Airlines had a scheduled flight taking off the next morning and could reach Lanzhou the next day. The woman was overjoyed upon hearing the news and immediately bought a ticket and returned to school to pack her luggage. There was a student named Ling who was also one of the pursuers of the lady on weekdays. At that time, he learned about the matter and bought a ticket to go there before the woman the next day. When the woman boarded, she saw Ling sitting side by side and asked in surprise where she was going. Ling smiled and said: Knowing that you are forced by filial piety, flying alone for thousands of miles, I specially came to be a follower. The woman initially thought it was a joke, but when she saw that his words were sincere and the ticket he was holding pointed to the same place as her own, she suddenly felt that there was a companion on the journey and was quite interested. When the plane took off, Ling diligently protected her and was meticulous in every way. Then the plane suddenly rose and fell, almost suspecting that she was in the midst of stormy waves. The woman was inevitably dizzy because it was her first flight. Ling became more protective and careful, and pointed out the sights and scenes along the way to encourage her. The woman gradually felt at ease and had more fun. That night, she stayed at the Xi'an Northwest Hotel. The woman missed her mother's illness and turned over all night. When the night was about to end, she still saw a figure wandering outside the window and recognized it as Ling. She called out and asked why she didn't sleep. Ling Yun: The inn is lonely and quiet. I am afraid that you are afraid of insomnia, so I specially patrol remotely. The woman couldn't bear it very much and urged her to go to bed frequently. Ling responded slowly. The next day, Ling's eyes were all red because he hadn't slept all night. After arriving in Lanzhou, the woman went home with Ling. Her mother's illness had improved slightly. In addition to being happy, she deeply felt Ling's thousands of miles of following and became more cordial. After returning to school, she made a marriage contract with him. Recently, the reporter went to Ping for some business and happened to attend their wedding banquet. The guests were shocked by the bride's beauty and asked to announce the history of their marriage. Ling Sheng then happily recounted the process as described above. The woman's surname is Huo, and her father is an industrialist, a descendant of General Huo Qubing of the Han Dynasty. (Thank you)

Manifestations of National Character 166

— Moon

Records of Floating Incense 167

— Original by Princess Der Ling, Translated by Qin Shouou

Because that Governor of the Province, after receiving the imperial decree, was sent to Heilongjiang as a soldier, he soon died there; although his family was still safely left in his hometown, his property had been confiscated by the Empress Dowager, and at most only the daily needs of the family could be maintained. In addition, everyone knew that they were the family members of criminals and could not help but despise them. Not only could they not get rich again, but they would lose face everywhere.

I remember two or three years ago, which was more than 20 years after the demise of the Manchu Qing Dynasty. I was in Shanghai. One day, I accidentally walked into a silk company and selected several pieces of clothing material. Since it was inconvenient to carry them back myself, I wrote down my name and address and asked them to send someone to deliver them to me. In the evening, they sent a very low-level clerk to deliver the things. But this person was very strange. After I received the things, he didn't just go out. He blushed and asked me:

"Has the madam lived in the palace before?"

This question was of course very surprising to me, but I really didn't need to hide it, so I immediately nodded in agreement. Then he continued to tell me that he himself was also a son of an official family and had been a family friend with my family, but for more than 20 years, he had been in a very difficult situation, and everyone around him was mocking him, making it impossible for them to have a future, so he himself was reduced to being a clerk in a silk shop because he had no other choice.

When I heard him say his surname, I suddenly understood. It turned out that he was the youngest son of the evil governor who was sent to Heilongjiang by the Empress Dowager; I didn't expect that more than 20 years had passed, and the just punishment that the Empress Dowager gave to the rebel minister had not failed, and it was still like it had just happened yesterday! (379)

World Rare News

The World's Attention on Quintuplets 168

— Special

In Ontario, Canada, the wife of a resident named Dionne gave birth to quintuplets last year. During labor, the process was naturally very difficult. Fortunately, the renowned Dr. Dafoe's surgery was highly skilled, and all five babies were safely delivered. The mother also remained safe and sound. Babies born as quintuplets are naturally weaker than ordinary infants, so it was extremely difficult to raise them in the first few months. However, with special care from doctors, each of them grew up to be adorable. They are now over a year old. Originally, the Ontario government, considering quintuplets a rare occurrence in the world and fearing inadequate care from their parents, which would jeopardize their safety, obtained the consent of the parents immediately after the babies were born and placed them under state care. A highly sanitary nursery was built not far from the parents' residence, and Mrs. Kirilenko, a dedicated caregiver, along with several assistants, was hired to provide specialized care. Two capable policemen were also assigned to guard them day and night to prevent any unexpected harm.

The Dionne couple's family was originally poor. Recently, some people have been trying to persuade them to take back the quintuplets from the authorities to make money. Eighty percent of the profits would go to the Dionne couple, with the manager taking the remaining ten percent. They even said to the Dionne couple: "If you had a gold mine, would the government be able to seize it? Naturally, they would allow you to mine it as you please. Then, how can the government have the right to take away your five children?" Mr. Croll, the Minister of Public Welfare in Ontario, and his colleagues disagreed with this. Mr. Croll said, "These five children cannot be compared to a gold mine. This is an unprecedented event in scientific history. Canada regards it as a national treasure, and the government has a sacred duty to protect these five little treasures who are related to the world, and to prevent them from being exploited and endangering their safety. Under no circumstances can we allow them to leave their current sanitary residence and be displayed as oddities for people to see."

Since the quintuplets were born, they caused a sensation across the country. Furthermore, the quintuplets were born lively and adorable, so people from all walks of life hoped to see them and feast their eyes. Initially, after consultation with the guardians, it was agreed that people could watch them through the glass window from 2:00 PM to 3:00 PM every Sunday afternoon. After this news spread, everyone rushed to be first, and each time, there were always four or five hundred people coming to see them. However, viewing is no longer permitted now because these nine children can now understand things. They see many strangers crowding outside the window, looking and talking noisily, and they also open their small eyes wide, staring outward. As a result, they experience neurological reactions at night when they sleep, making them quite restless. Therefore, Dr. Dafoe ordered that people should not be allowed to watch them even on Sundays. At the same time, anything that could harm the well-being of the quintuplets is strictly prohibited. However, the quintuplets' parents can still visit them freely. Their mother can play with the quintuplets and help with bathing and dressing them. Currently, the quintuplets' bodies are very healthy, but according to Dr. Dafoe's opinion, the quintuplets were all born prematurely, so in the coming months, they still need special care to ensure everything goes smoothly.

These five children can now babble and crawl on the ground. They spend their days together, playing with each other, and seeing their comical state makes people stand for hours without getting bored. Their faces are similar, making it easy to mistake them. They wake up in bed at five o'clock every morning, singing and playing with their small hands, and making sounds from their throats, as if urging the caregivers to change their clothes. They bathe once in the morning and evening, playing and splashing in the water. After eating, they change their clothes and are placed in a stroller in the hallway by the caregivers, allowing them to play or sleep. They eat again at noon, and by seven o'clock in the evening, they all fall asleep. According to the current caregiver, Mrs. Kirilenko, these five children are very humorous. If you give them something they don't like to eat, they will pretend to be sick. They often look at you out of the corner of their eyes to see if you are paying attention to them. If you go to hug them, they will laugh heartily and throw themselves into your arms, which is truly lovely!

These five children are fortunate to have Dr. Dafoe, whose surgery skills are superb, deliver them, and a government that values the well-being of children to carefully care for them. Otherwise, we often hear of single births, but the babies always die soon after birth, or die within a few days. To raise quintuplets to be healthy in every way is undoubtedly a miracle in the world.

Little Western Paradise 169

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seventeen: Do Not Ask a Daughter’s Difficulties; Unspeakable Pain is Hidden. Let Us All Strive to Behold the Face of a Noble Person and Admire Their Lofty Character.

While drinking tea, he twitched his eyebrows twice, then put down his teacup and smiled, saying, "In Mr. Cheng’s opinion, how is this matter?" Zhichian said, "I have a joke that can be used as an analogy. I heard that the ghost of someone who died unjustly must find a replacement..." Before Huanhua could finish speaking, she blushed and smiled, "Yes, in order to make his match successful, Mr. Jia helped me with train fare so that I could return to Jiangnan, as if catching this Miss Zhu as a replacement. In fact, this Miss Cai has no choice but to marry. Even if I didn't act as a matchmaker, she would still marry someone. Moreover, what was I doing in Xi'an? She now has a master and doesn't have to worry about food or clothing, which is very different from my situation." Zhichian looked at him for a long time without saying a word. He felt that on her skin, which usually didn't wear makeup, a flush was showing. He thought of Yueying's face, which, in its healthy color, revealed a hint of pallor. That's how things are in the world, always opposing and complementing each other. Huanhua, seeing him staring like that, felt a little embarrassed and forced herself to calm down, saying, "I know Mr. Cheng likes that girl very much, but when we came out to be matchmakers, you never said you wanted her." Zhichian waved his hands repeatedly and laughed, "Far from it, far from it! Let's drop this matter and not talk about it anymore." Huanhua took two more sips of tea, staring into the teacup, and then said, "I can't count myself as gone yet. There is a car going to Tongguan tomorrow, and Mr. Jia has arranged for someone to take me. He gave me a dozen or so dollars, which is only enough to buy a third-class train ticket, and maybe not even enough. Even if I don't eat or drink on the way, if anything small happens, I won't have any spare money to take out. How can I dare to leave boldly?" (279)

Foodstuffs 174

The Origin of the Saying About Opening Auctions for Foreign Wheat

Foreign Wheat Could Originally Be Received and Released, But Japanese Merchants Will Now Conduct Open Transactions

The claim that the Grain Exchange is opening auctions for foreign wheat is not factual. According to the Exchange's long-standing practice, foreign wheat has always been handled for delivery according to standard procedures. The grades of wheat from places like Canada and Australia are also reviewed and determined annually. Therefore, there is no need to establish separate standards. In reality, it's a return to the old practice, where foreign wheat transported by Japanese ships and stored in Japanese warehouses can be received and released as usual without rejection. This means the secret of Japanese merchants hawking foreign wheat is now out in the open.

Chips Will Increase, the Flour and Wheat Market Is Quite Volatile

The flour market has turned weak. Foreign wheat quotations fluctuate up and down within two days, but are still up by about 35 cents overall. Market sentiment is quite uneasy. Initially, rumors of inflation were considered unlikely to materialize. Then, it was thought that transportation costs for foreign wheat shipped by Eastern vessels might be lower. As a result, market sentiment has loosened, and opening prices have fallen by 1.01 cents compared to the closing price at the end of last month. For January deliveries, the market has shown an inverted pattern, because inland factories in the Yangtze River region start to join the standard, expanding the chips. However, speaking practically, this view may not hold true. Subsequent trading in all contracts remains active, with most bulls frequently unloading their positions and sometimes going short, causing market sentiment to waver. Foreign wheat bids have reached around $5.00 due to exchange rate issues, so the outlook seems cautiously optimistic. As a result, this month's price fell by 1.25 cents, September's fell by 2 cents, October's fell by 1 cent, November/December's fell by 1.25 cents, and January's opening price was 45 cents with a closing price of 6 cents, showing a gain of 1 cent.

The wheat market has seen a sharp drop in opening prices for all months. Although foreign wheat quotations have shown improvement, market sentiment is downbeat due to the unconfirmed inflation rumors and the talk of opening auctions for foreign wheat. Therefore, after the opening prices, market sentiment for all months has been weak, especially for the current month, as customers with inventory frequently hedged, leading to unstable positions. For distant months, prices are relatively favorable due to contracts with Eastern merchants for foreign wheat, causing a somewhat subdued sentiment. However, this is currently just speculation and may not reflect reality. As a result, this month's price fell by 8 cents from the end of last month, September/October's fell by 6 cents, and November's fell by 5 cents.

The Spot Wheat Market: High-quality wheat is unaffected by the standard, only intermediate wheat is slightly softer. Shandong Yaowan wheat opened at $3.64, Gaoyou wheat at $3.59, Jiangyan wheat at $3.57, and Danyang wheat at $3.53. Xinda shipped out 4,500 bags, and Fufeng shipped out 2,000 bags.

Local and Foreign Rice Sales Are Brisk, Prices Are Up

Local rice (from South Shanghai) saw limited arrivals from brokers yesterday, with only ten-odd firms (totaling over 2,000 piculs). This led to increased bullishness. Sales on the local street were quite brisk, creating a tight situation and a positive market sentiment. Prices for various grades of thick粳 (jīng) rice rose by 10-20 cents, and there was continued demand for various grades of thin秈 (xiān) rice. Brokers from Qingdao, Yantai, and Qinhuangdao purchased over 400 bags, with sluggish retail sales. Prices increased by 10 cents to over 10 cents. Dongxin (東新) led with 2-尺 (chǐ) rice, and芦尖 (lú jiān) rice remained fresh. The market on the north side of the river was unaffected by陰變元 (yīn biàn yuán).

Local rice saw 11-12 firms arriving from various routes. There were 40-50 boats docked at 河下 (Héxià). Sales of various types of white粳 (jīng) rice were brisk due to low inventory in stores. Retail sales were quite active, and prices suddenly jumped by 30-40 cents. Arrivals of early稻 (dào) rice were low but sales were active, and prices followed suit with a 20-30 cent increase. After early薄稻 (báo dào) rice sold out, the market tightened. There was little inventory of 白元河 (bái yuán hé) rice, and retail sales were average. However, buyers were quite firm, causing prices to increase by 20-30 cents. Other types of rice also showed tightening. Dongxin粳 (jīng) rice has been strong for several days, with approximately 500 piculs sold, and retail sales were active, with prices rising by 20 cents.

The foreign rice market was quite lively yesterday. As it was learned that the city's foreign rice inventory was dwindling and orders had all been fulfilled, and with gold prices high and legal goods unprofitable, both sellers and hoarders were setting high bids. Market sentiment was upward. Yesterday, buyers were very eager, with Jiujiang actively buying first, followed by Nanjing, and local streets and hoarders were even more active. Morning prices immediately jumped by 15 cents. In the afternoon, local buyers continued to be active, with inquiries coming not only from the three aforementioned areas but also from inland and northern regions. Rice prices continued to jump by another 10 cents, resulting in a significant increase of 20-30 cents compared to the previous day. Transaction volumes were also higher than usual, with 17,500 bags of Saigon rice, 7,000 bags of Xiaojiao (小絞) rice, and 5,000 bags of Sujing, Dimindang, and Siamese rice. The total volume was close to 30,000 bags, and sentiment remained optimistic. If local buying continues to be strong, prices may gradually increase.

Scarce Arrival of New Jiangxi Soybeans Causes Market to Rise

Since the arrival of new Jiangxi soybeans on the market, arrivals have been scarce, with only a few dozen bags per batch, leading to a supply shortage. As a result, market sentiment has trended upward. Yesterday, two shipments of Jiangqiao (江橋) soybeans arrived, totaling only 99 bags, priced at $3.84, up 4 cents from the previous batch. 66 bags of 城門 (Chéngmén) soybeans were priced at $4.00, up 10 cents, but the quality was better than the previous batch. The goods were still being purchased by Ningbo merchants, and local streets had demand but no goods. If no substantial shipments arrive in the future, the market is likely to improve.

Sugar Market: Hainan Brown Sugar Opening Prices Tighten

Yesterday, the sugar market trended steady. There was little change in the prices of granulated and refined sugar, as well as Taikoo sugar and native cotton white sugar in public board quotations. However, over 2,800 bags of domestic Hainan brown sugar, previously offered at lower prices, had been sold, and brokers showed strong interest. The market gradually saw a turnaround, with reports of prices rising by 20-30 cents in open trading and some transactions in after-hours trading.

Silk and Tea: Luxiang Zhenmei Continues to Trend Firm and Rise

Sales of Luxiang and Zhenmei green tea continued to be brisk. Yesterday, companies such as Yingzhuang, Xiehe, Jinlong, Tongfu, and Fushi continued to make every effort to purchase. Total transaction volume for Zhenmei, Xiaomu, Mazhu, Zhenmei, Gongxi, and other items reached over 4,300 boxes. High-quality Zhenmei was priced as high as $95-96, up $2-3 from previous levels, and other items also showed a generally firm trend. However, the black tea market remained stagnant, with particularly sluggish sales of medium and low-grade teas from areas such as Lianghu and Ningzhou.

North-South Goods: Preserved Mustard Tuber Sales Rebound, Rising $2

Since the introduction of new Sichuan preserved mustard tubers, sales have been slow, leading to occasional price declines. It was found that the lowest opening price for sub-grade goods was no more than $8. Specializing merchants, who had previously suffered significant losses, took the opportunity to replenish their stocks. However, buyers have also sold over 10,000 jars of goods before and after, leaving approximately 12,000 jars in inventory. Yesterday, the market saw a $2 increase in opening prices.

Free Talk Miscellaneous Essays "The Decameron" by Mengjia

In 14th-century Italy, the economic situation had far surpassed that of Dante's time. Especially in Florence, the economic relations of this nascent capitalist era were particularly pronounced, giving rise to new social groups such as craftsmen, merchants, sailors, and other small urban property owners. The establishment of a new Italian culture meant that the medieval poetic style, Dante's "Divine Comedy"—with its idealistic symbolism, intense asceticism, and the belief that "earthly life is a valley of sorrow and sin, and all earthly things are baseless. The meaning and purpose of life lie in the negation of all earthly things, in religion, in the contemplation of God"—and the solemn figures of the great teachers of the Church and the founders of monasteries that flickered within it, were no longer suitable for the growth of new content and were replaced by prose novels. In this sense, Boccaccio's "Decameron" naturally replaced the position of the "Divine Comedy."

Of course, we must not overlook the features of the "Divine Comedy," created by Dante in the growing new cultural environment—such as taking "individuality" as the center of life, and its unrestrained and absurd dreamlike quality, which was the opposite of medieval poetry, and the sprouts of realistic creative methods that were revealed in this solemn symbolic idealistic artistic composition, etc. However, Dante's "Divine Comedy," in its main content, is still a spiritual form of expression of human society at the end of the Middle Ages, a record of the spiritual and soul life. It depicts emperors, kings, knights, saints, praises the spirit of asceticism, extremely despises all carnal pleasures, believes that earthly desires are sinful, and still sincerely admires and praises the "sublime" of hypocritical monks. From this, we can say without exaggeration that Dante's "Divine Comedy" is a poem of feudal religious culture.

In contrast, Boccaccio, the first person in the history of Italian realistic literature, boldly declares in his "Decameron" that carnal pleasure is a natural right of mankind, sings the praises of matter and carnal desire, and is convinced that those who believe that they are divorced from all worldly things as soon as they put on a cassock are just "fools." He opposes the asceticism of the Church with the doctrine that carnal pleasure is a natural right of mankind. He bitterly ridicules the hypocrisy of the foolish monastic society, portraying them as deceivers and "stupid philistines." He portrays these "red-faced, extremely fat, crowing like roosters, walking proudly with their chests puffed out, steeped in sin even to their ears, yet putting on the face of the master of heaven and dividing up places in heaven and the blessings of the Lord according to the amount of money" "noble" monks as laughable figures, like those clowns in China today who put on powder on their noses but wear long beards and pretend to be old men singing high-pitched tunes. He peels off the masks of the monks—who verbally advocate asceticism, praising it to the skies, but secretly hide wine and various spices in their rooms—giving them fatal and biting satire. He describes the temperament of those merchants who became rich from poverty, full of adventurous spirit and vigor, describes the worldly psychology of these new social classes, and their carnal and material daily life. All the characters in his works, regardless of their status, are excited and feel the joy of new life because of their physical health and worldly pleasures—here we can hear "the healthy laughter of those who live in material satisfaction, who are freed from the oppression of dark phantoms and painful remorse, who do not pin their hopes on gods and angels. But rely entirely on their own intelligence, invention, their own ability and adventurous heart," in short, on their own full and vibrant vitality in opening up new avenues of life. This laughter of joy arising from feeling the joy of life, like the crowing of a rooster at dawn, announces the coming of a new era. In this respect, the tone of "The Decameron" is completely different from the lyrical elegy of the "Divine Comedy," typically expressing the feelings of two classes with completely different fates.

Regarding the form of "The Decameron," we can say that it is base, that is, in the artistic sense, it is incomplete and trivial. In the one hundred stories, although the themes are diverse and rich, it uses a speaking storytelling method, so in the process of story development and its artistic composition, it lacks a sense of integrity and architecture. The characters of the protagonists are not obvious, flat, and not vivid, and the psychological descriptions are not profound. Therefore, although Boccaccio declared the birth of a new social stratum in "The Decameron," he did not perfectly depict the typical characters of this new character. At this point, Boccaccio only abstractly and plainly expressed the worldview of an emerging social group without concretely expressing the entire attitude of these new types in their real life, in their active actions, and in their inner spiritual life. This may be the most important reason. However, Boccaccio's use and deepening of the earlier Italian "extremely short stories with fantastic content" and making it establish its position in the history of Italian literature, and its advocacy of taking the self as the center, and using "realistic events and realistic characters" that do not contain symbolic meaning at all to replace the previous religious longing for "heaven" and the abstract allegorical characters in the poems of fantasy, he can be said to be the first old realist writer. Here, we emphasize Boccaccio's greatness not so much for his amazing formal refinement, elegance, and artistic completeness, but rather for the epoch-making nature of his creative methods, for his being the first old realist writer, for his being the first person to open up realistic literature in Italy and even Europe.

Passing Dantu at Night by Shen Shengshi

The train let out a hoarse roar, climbing out of the tunnel.

A night scene of a mountain village.

Rows of dark, oppressive thatched cottages lined the hillside. Occasionally, one or two points of amber light leaked from the wooden plank windows of the cottages.

In the deep, quiet midnight, the sound of frogs, like striking a fragile drum, seeped up from the grassy ponds of the village.

A piece of cloud, like delicately folded gauze, embraced a crescent moon. The moon led a group of lively stars, leisurely and slowly traveling across the sky.

The train, like a giant monster, panted and roared, climbing across a quiet and secluded countryside.

The surging river water, churning with waves; the quiet moonlight reflecting on the river, a distant patch of light, leaping like a candle flame in the heart of the water.

I gazed intently, at the early summer night scene outside the train window. The train carried my heart, gliding across the quiet, moonlit countryside.

Striking a paper cigarette, I silently savored the quiet taste of the night. The crescent moon quietly ascended to the mid-sky. When I looked out the window again, the plains of Dantu had already flown past the train window.

In the Gambling Den by Li Sanlang

——One of the Sketches of the Oriental Monte Carlo

Arrogant, this place is filled with a tense and stifling atmosphere. Although Macau relies on the vast sea coast, and a row of gambling den flags flutter in the sea breeze, once you step into the gambling den, it feels like being buried in hell, without enjoying any fresh air.

Inside, white, glaring lights are hung high, dazzling. However, because the people in the place are diligently or patiently smoking cigarettes, puffs of white-gray smoke rings spread upwards, filling the small hall. It makes people suspect that this is not a human world, but a world of demons.

People, mixed together, some dressed like elegant young men or wealthy merchants, while others wear only tattered clothes, mixing together without distinction, surrounding the rectangular tables. It's as if a group of hungry lambs are waiting for someone to stuff food into their mouths, their eyes wide with wild desire. Their faces are constantly jumping and convulsing, moving with the second hand of the clock.

In the summer, there are fierce electric fans, but no matter what, in the sunless southern gambling den, it is always depressing and fiery. People sweat, but their eyes are fixed on the action of the dealers, or on the money or banknotes on the square grids of the table. It's as if they have forgotten their own lives, sacrificing themselves entirely to the authority of money, which is like a sword.

In the winter, although there are no heaters, if you wear thick clothes and come in, you will always be unable to bear the stuffiness and heat and want to take your clothes off. Indeed, this place is always the same, a kind of heat that is not from the sun but a terrible stifling atmosphere.

There is no distinction between day and night here. There are only patient gamblers, perhaps burying their heads in the gambling den from morning. The emissaries of money will have soaked their heads with an anesthetic, and they will continuously, tirelessly, endure through the day and into the dark night. The clock hanging on the wall seems to have become a false shadow, and no real gambler ever notices the passage of time. In this way, they endure through the day and the night. Although they win ten or a hundred times their capital, no matter how suddenly they become rich, they still greedily, forgetting their own lives, sink down until all the money has safely slipped into the hands of others. Only then, with curses and remorse in their hearts, weary bodies, and confused heads, do they hobble out of the threshold. They then try to find some money, even if it means selling their wives and children, all sacrificed for the desire to gamble. Some clever gamblers, when they win a large sum of money here, run to the circles of glamorous women, intoxicating their lives. When they have no possibility of living, they quietly jump into the black sea. Or become gangsters. In reality, no one who comes here has a good outcome, only immersing one's life in poison.

The Oriental Monte Carlo of Macau is forever spinning like this without stopping!

A Corner of the Taihang Mountains (Part 1) by Lu Fen

The weather is clear, with two or three white clouds moving in the distant mountains. The mountain color is verdant, making the white of the clouds incomparably beautiful. The sunlight happily shines on the mountains, forests, villages. The dew of last night has not yet completely dissipated. The water carrier puts the bucket into the pond, making a gurgling sound, splashing clear water droplets. The wife washes clothes by the pond, chatting and laughing. The child drives the sheep up the mountain, constantly cracking the whip. The donkey occasionally brays loudly, and piglets waddle past on the roadside. All around is such a sweet, quiet, and peaceful scene, intoxicating!

The person called "Old Brother" took me to the small mountain at the end of the town. Needless to say, I had many strange ideas, listening to him greet the residents along the way.

Reaching the top of the mountain, "Old Brother" was still standing at the foot of the mountain, chatting with someone. That person was about forty years old, with a shaved head, wearing a gray robe, and carrying a pistol at his side. It was unclear what kind of person he was. Not like a thug, nor like a gentleman, but he had a shiny gold tooth, and was considered elegant among the residents. Not far behind him stood a young man, his face shaved like a freshly cut lawn, but his complexion was dark and lackluster. He was very handsome, and seemed like he could race with wolves if he shouted. His eyes were blank, emitting a cruel light, indicating that he was about to kill or be killed. He looked as agile as a small beast. He carried a German "Monk's Cap" rifle on his shoulder, and I was reminded of soldiers in the trenches.

The man calmly took off his rifle and fired a shot without any purpose. This seemed like a normal thing. A group of porters were passing by him, the bells ringing dong-dong, the mules and donkeys shook their big ears, and the drivers continued to crack their whips. The water carriers swayed their bodies, and clear water splashed on the ground. No one bothered to look at the gunshot and walked past.

According to "Old Brother," the person he was talking to was a landlord. The three brothers lived separately. One night, the eldest brother's family of eight were all slaughtered by a former district chief, simply because of a small ancestral grievance. Now they had moved to this town, and that man was his tenant and bodyguard.

University Days (36) by Storm, translated by Chen Yinzi

I also saw the 'Count of Dithmarschen', looking tired and sitting cross-legged on the other side of the hall. – I stood near him. When the musicians picked up their instruments, a young student came up to him. 'May I dance with Nellie this time?' he asked timidly. 'Next time, "youngster"!' the 'Count of Dithmarschen' replied, leaning his fine, pale head against the wall. The music began, but he did not stand up to invite his partner, only lazily raising his hand and gesturing to her with his fingers. I saw an angry look flash across her face, and then she hid her eyes inside the hand she was propping up, without standing up. The 'Count of Dithmarschen' frowned, and after a while got up, walked across the hall, and stood in front of her. – As she still did not look up, he put his arm around her and quickly lifted her up. He seemed to say two angry words, but I was standing too far away to hear them. Then he escorted her to the front of the other couples and began to dance.

She was already a tall girl, but her head only reached his chest. I watched them for a long time; her head was tilted back, her body seemingly only supported by his arm, only her toes touching the floor; he looked down at her, his hawk-like eyes fixed on her face, which was closed against him. After the dance, he took her back to her seat and let her gently slide from his arms onto the chair.

This rest was not long. Soon the whole hall was in commotion, the music played a quick tune, and the dancers quickly lined up in pairs.

The dancing began again, laughter and raucous shouts filling the entire circle; I saw those light little feet sliding quickly again and again over those dark spots. Faster and faster, and at the last spin, the poor children would have fallen to the ground, for they were spinning too fast.

Then, the music stopped abruptly; the dancing girls blushed and got up from the floor as the students laughed and walked away over their bodies, wiping the hair from their foreheads or shaking the dust off their carefully-made dancing dresses. I don't know whether this was due to the remnants of childish mischief or to the instinctive movement of all people to show resistance to something they cannot escape the magic of? It seemed that these college students did not think they had sufficiently insulted the women.

My eyes never left Nellie. They sat alone in the place where the 'Count of Dithmarschen' had taken her. She seemed to suppress herself so that no one invited her to dance in that dance.

After a while, people solemnly and deliberately danced the 'contre-danse', as if intentionally indicating the opposite nature of that dance. At this time I went into the side room with an acquaintance. We met many old students, and soon a glass of beer was placed in front of everyone, and we talked a great deal about what the results of this exam might be.

When the music next door stopped, several couples came up to us and sat down at the table. The 'Count of Dithmarschen' and Nellie were among them.

Summer Scene on the Street: Calling "Brother" by Tianji

Essays and Education by Qinwen

If literature is indeed "cultivation," and essays at least have a large part of the elements of literature, then its relationship with education is not a problem. Moreover, within the scope of literature, the relationship between essays and education is closer than that of novels and plays. Not to mention anything else, just check the textbooks and selected readings, no matter which bookstore publishes them, you can see that the number of essays is greater than that of novels and plays. In classical Chinese, many "miscellaneous sayings" are always selected. This is certainly because essays are short and clever, making it easy for students to understand and feel interested, and also because essays are refined, every sentence has force, and every place is outstanding and eye-catching, which can unconsciously arouse students' desire to try. Unlike novels and plays, which require reading the entire long piece to understand the intention, if only a part is read, some places are inevitably inexplicable and feel ordinary and tasteless. In the classroom, it is inconvenient to read long works in one breath, so essays occupy a superior position.

The above is only about textbooks. In fact, essays are also suitable for extracurricular reading; simple and clear, easy for self-study; gentle and moving, after reading a little, one will naturally be reluctant to put it down. "Historical essays" and "scientific essays" are not only beneficial in writing but also useful for various subjects and can be called a powerful tool for "supplementary education." Moreover, it is even more beneficial to "social education," which can be understood from the large number of essays published in general newspapers and magazines.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Speaking of Shanghai Hosting the Ghost Festival Again by Xing An

The seventh lunar month has arrived again, and Shanghai people are making a fuss about holding the Ghost Festival. Shanghai people live in this unique commercial hub in the country, taking the lead in the world's trends. Logically, customs should change a bit. The change to the Gregorian calendar has been rigorously implemented by the government for several years, but Shanghai people still feign compliance while actually disobeying, celebrating their lunar New Year. National Day and days of national humiliation can be skipped over, but when it comes to welcoming gods and holding festivals, they cannot help but happily participate. Now that the time for the Ghost Festival has arrived, Shanghai people will inevitably be busy again, holding grand Taoist rituals. These days, a bunch of idle people in Shanghai are actively going around collecting money from house to house, promoting the grand event. The streets and alleys are also decorated with lanterns and colored banners, preparing for the excitement. The superstitious beliefs of Shanghai people are truly unbreakable.

Naturally, Shanghai people have their own incredibly foolish intentions for holding the Ghost Festival, which is to pray for the peace of the area. But as I see it, the peace of Shanghai is already as peaceful as it can be. Currently, the provinces are suffering from major floods, and hundreds of thousands of disaster victims are in dire straits, crying out to heaven and earth. This kind of unpeaceful scene is enough to make you feel sad and miserable! However, Shanghai people are probably indifferent to this, not concerned at all.

The other day, Mr. Ma Xiangbo issued an appeal to the people of the country to save and help disaster victims, pleading for the lives of the disaster victims. I believe that there will not be many people in the country who can truly mobilize their compassion, save on clothing and food, and generously donate. Because this directly affects personal life. It would be a truly meritorious act if Shanghai people saved the useless waste of holding Taoist rituals this month and donated it to the disaster area to help rescue the victims! Saving living people is much more charitable than saving dead people. However, my proposal is also a kind of extravagant hope? Maybe Shanghai people are mostly determined to save the Taoist rituals at all costs, even if the disaster victims go unsaved.

Then there is a need to ban this bad custom. Yesterday, I heard that the Social Affairs Bureau believes that holding the Ghost Festival in this city is promoting superstition and wasting money and manpower to the extreme. At a time when the provinces are suffering from terrible floods and the disaster victims are waiting for help, how can we use the money earned with blood and sweat for useless consumption? We should find ways to ban it to reverse the decadent trend. It was reported that officials had been sent to consult with the Public Security Bureau a few days ago. In addition to the two bureaus jointly issuing a notice, the Public Security Bureau will also issue orders to all subordinates to strictly prohibit it. Let's see what the state of the Shanghai Public Ritual for Peace will be this year.

The Knife Sharpener by Cun Yin

My little knife was rusty.

Because I didn’t have time to sharpen it, I asked an old scissors sharpener to do the job for me.

The old man’s clothes were tattered, like the dried fur of a stray dog running wild on the street with no home to go to. His face was covered with veins. The gray stubble under his chin moved with the two red and white lips. Judging from his two lifeless eyes, I really didn’t know how much misfortune he had suffered.

After he accepted my little knife, he straddled his narrow, dirty stool. He looked at the knife carefully, frowned his two old eyebrows, and said with great difficulty:

"Sir, seven copper coins, please! It's really not easy to sharpen.”

This sentence was clearly intended to ask me for a few more coins. His attitude was very sincere, very timid. Perhaps because of his pitiful appearance, I agreed without hesitation.

"The steel of this knife is very good, sir!"

With a smile on his face, he spoke to me so diligently that I felt embarrassed. "Why be like this, old man? I'm taking out money, and you're expending effort! Why be so ingratiating? Our exchange is so fair..." I wanted to say this to him, but some kind of consciousness stopped me. I had to return a smile on my face to him.

So, on a brick, it resonated with a "Kagukagu" sound. (The sound of my little knife hovering above it).

His dry muscles, bare chest, several bones, and yellow skin all wriggled with the strange, piercing sound of "Kagukagu". I seemed to see an old, outdated machine.

Standing next to him, watching this living machine moving back and forth, I became a little impatient. I saw a small, round hole in his ear, which was very strange, so I asked him:

"The hole in your ear, it's really strange.”

"Yes, it's been four or five years." His painful voice had no long breath. His pitiful eyes turned to look at me, then he cast his eyes on the little knife that his hands were pushing. Then, he murmured to himself towards the little knife hovering on the brick: "That year, the place where I lived started to have war. -- Sir, we Jiangbei people have too many hard lives. -- Soldiers passed in rows in front of my thatched house. Later, we heard the sound of guns and cannons. Later, we saw the red light all over the sky, and the surrounding houses, and our row of thatched houses, were all burned down by the soldiers. We ran for our lives! We wanted to escape this terrible place. We stepped on the still groaning corpses. Our shoes were soaked with the blood flowing on the ground. We ran for our lives! It was at that time that a stray bullet passed through my ear. At that time, I didn’t feel any pain at all, and when I rested and hid in a ditch, I realized that the clothes on my shoulder were soaked with blood..."

His hands stopped, and his head also lifted up. He looked at me sternly and said frantically:

"It would have been better to die at that time, sir. It would have saved me from such suffering."

"You are so lucky, you still have the strength, you will not suffer.” I could only comfort him like this. Apart from this, what else could I say? Although there was so much to say, some kind of consciousness stopped me again. It was too painful, I couldn't say my words directly.

The "Kagukagu" sound slowed down. He had sharpened my little knife very brightly and sharply.

"Is this good, sir? Such a fast knife, can kill many of our enemies."

"Do you also understand enemies?" I said ironically.

He smiled bitterly, without answering.

I paid him seven copper coins, and he carried his stool on his back, carried endless pain. We all parted with bitter smiles. Parted!

The Suffering Woman by Jian Bi

Her internal experience of ten years in the nunnery was even more important than her chanting and worship. Previously, she had not revered any religious thoughts, but now she considered it utter absurdity because "utter absurdity" had given rise to the desire to "repent and do good." She was now praying, practicing asceticism, and repenting to seek salvation. But human will is ultimately weak and cannot withstand strong temptations. After ten years without incident, in the eleventh year, she was thrown out of the door of asceticism and enlightenment as if being punished by God.

"No matter how strong your will is, you can't overcome natural impulses!" Martin Luther's words once again accurately told her the inevitability of her behavior.

Living in a fluctuating environment, the cold and warm tastes of twenty years of life were mostly occupied by the bitterness in her memories. For her own inexplicable life history, each page was splattered with blood and tears, and each page was absurd.

Unbearable loneliness forced her to rationally believe in religion. The chanting and worship in the incense mist of her ancestors and mothers now made her laugh at their cleverness and whip herself for being foolish. The grandfather's concubine and the father's extramarital affair were originally the "reasons for belief in God" of the ancestors and mothers. As for herself, it was more accurate to say that she felt empty because she loved too much!

Page 20

However, the nunnery was ultimately a sacred Buddhist site. The desperate attempt to restrain emotions by entrusting them to the wooden fish could not last. She understood the reason for this. Then she remembered a certain story about why a male gardener had been the target of many nuns. The still lake of her heart began to ripple.

On a clear moonlit night, when the silvery moonlight kissed the shadows of the trees on the ground, when the amorous god of spring night descended with light wings, she gently chanted a famous poem:

"Power and life have flown far away,

Friends are gone, joy is dead;

The honor that once nourished me is also gone,

Belief is on my weak star.

The time of people's short lives is fruitless.

All the good things that life has given me

Are the floods of tears that comfort my heart,

All things must return to dust,

Except for that neat, beautiful, and secluded thing – nature's spring night."

Like the realism, moving, and magical descriptions in novels, a head poked out from the dark corner of the house, whispering:

"Darling, let's go! It's almost time, the train is already rolling its wheels, listen..."

Two shadows were printed in horror on the moonlit earth. The man's hat moved like a small umbrella under the moon.

From then on, she was once again covered in the dust of the world.

After Today I Am Going to Close the Store (One of the Features) by Qin Jian

The weather is getting hot like fire, and the cicadas are screaming like slaughtering pigs on the branches again. At this time, in a metropolis filled with countless souls seeking a living, on the walls of street corners, mixed in with posters for menstrual pills and theater advertisements, a pile of small and crooked autumn enrollment advertisements for "alleyway elementary schools" will appear again. They are posted and distributed everywhere, using moving and accommodating words such as "popular education, reduced tuition fees, enrollment at any time" to replace the store's "preferential treatment for customers, small profits and quick sales."

So, walking on the street, walking in the prosperous area of residences and shops, in street after street, among the signs of doctors or fortune-tellers, it is easy to find the sign of an elementary school. There, the nearby residents, those living a not-so-comfortable life, will send their children to become part of the clientele under the principles of proximity, convenience, and economy, paying tuition fees of six or seven yuan per semester. There they are being educated, being guided, being formed, like a piece of wood that is left (no, entrusted) in an inferior carpenter's shop, lacking nutrition and care, drifting and growing up.

In any alleyway that is "prosperous and conveniently located," after a little calculation, one can rent a residential house and let the living room serve as the principal's office, the two厢房 (xiāngfáng) rooms upstairs and downstairs are divided into four classrooms (maybe you want to run a complete elementary school? But it doesn't matter, you can adopt the "multiple-grade education method" and implement "combined classes"), and the upper and lower亭子間 (tíngzijiān) rooms are used as the dormitories for the principal and teachers. Yarn and Cotton 175

Yarn: Marked Yarn Experiences Drastic Drop 176

The yarn market continues to decline, showing signs of instability. Fluctuations are frequent, making it difficult to predict. This situation is entirely due to the wavering minds of speculators who alternately buy and sell. According to market rumors, some large positions have been released recently, leading followers to rush to close their positions. At the same time, the spot yarn market is becoming increasingly quiet, and the market is falling more and more sharply.

Golden Rooster Plummets by More Than Two Dollars

At the opening of the marked yarn market, due to the massive purchases by peers the previous day, the sentiment was extremely bullish. The near-term contract rose by more than one dollar, and the distant contract rose by seventy or eighty cents. The situation in the second round remained tight, rising another seventy or eighty cents. By the third round, it was heard that spot yarn transactions were sluggish, and most transactions were for Japanese yarn. At the close, the market suddenly plummeted. The market situation changed drastically, because the person in charge of a certain party profited from releasing their own long positions of 1,000-2,000 bales. When the news broke, people were shaken, and followers rushed to close their positions. The market plunged by more than two dollars. As a result, the near-term contract rose by thirty cents compared to the previous day's close, while the distant contract fell by one dollar and fourteen cents. At the afternoon opening, the market remained weak. Rumors spread that the bulls were releasing positions, which was favorable to the bears, and Changfeng also began to dump a significant volume of over three thousand bales, causing the market to loosen significantly. As a result, the near-term contract fell by two dollars compared to the previous day, while the distant contract fell by eighty or ninety cents to one dollar and thirty cents. According to the investigation, the sellers included Da Feng with 1,000 bales, Tong Ji with 900 bales, Ming De with 1,200 bales, Zhen Da with 850 bales, He Xing with 500 bales, Ren Feng with 1,400 bales, Yong Chang with 900 bales, Yong Da with 600 bales, Chang Feng with 3,550 bales, and Run Kang with 1,100 bales, and Shen Yu with 700 bales. The buyers included Jin Chang with 1,800 bales, Da Ji with 900 bales, Shen Ji with 2,000 bales, Yi Chang with 2,450 bales, Run Kang with 700 bales, Geng Feng with 1,300 bales, and Rui Da with 400 bales. Spot Sales Only Exceed 500 Bales

Spot yarn sales are sluggish. According to statistics, various guilds purchased a total of 553 bales throughout the day. The purchase volume of each guild is as follows:

The cotton market is weakening, and the downward trend is intensifying. Because the bulls have been pushing up prices too aggressively for several days, they are now closing their positions when faced with unfavorable conditions, causing the downward trend to sharpen. However, large-scale bulls have not yet released their positions. Nevertheless, market rumors have subsided, and marked gold prices are stable. New buyers are temporarily stopping.

Zheng Marked Cotton Continues to Decline 177

At the opening of the marked cotton market, buyers gathered, because the bulls had been actively buying and adding to their positions the previous day, and their volumes were quite large, so they were bidding up prices even more aggressively. The current month broke through the six-dollar mark, and the distant months rose by twenty or thirty cents. By the second and third rounds, prices turned downward because rumors subsided and marked gold prices stabilized. As a result, prices for all months fell by one and a half to three cents compared to the previous day's close. In the afternoon, the bulls continued to close their positions, and sentiment was weak, with prices rising but then loosening. However, the bulls for the August contract remained strong. As a result, the current month fell by one and a half cents compared to the morning close, while the distant months fell by two and a half to three and a half cents. According to the investigation, the sellers included Tong He with 1,400 dan, Chang Feng with 1,500 dan, Tong Ji with 1,600 dan, Ji Feng with 1,400 dan, Ming De with 1,100 dan, Ren Feng with 2,000 dan, Yuan Yi with 1,000 dan, Sheng Yuan with 2,100 dan, Yong Chang with 4,600 dan, Yi Feng with 4,300 dan, and Chang He with 2,800 dan. The buyers included Chang Yu with 1,200 dan, Geng Feng with 1,500 dan, Yuan Da with 1,300 dan, Da Fu with 4,000 dan, Shen Chang with 1,400 dan, Rui Da with 1,800 dan, Shen Ji with 3,500 dan, Yi Chang with 3,300 dan, Chang Feng with 2,500 dan, Rui Yuan with 1,300 dan, and Yong Da with 1,400 dan. Factory Demand is Slightly Improving

Spot cotton sales are slightly more active. The sources include 236 bales of Yao cotton and 200 bales of Tongzhou cotton.

Good Forecast for New Tongzhou and Ningbo Cotton

"Tongzhou": This year's cotton crop in Tongzhou is expected to be abundant based on the current conditions. It is estimated that it can produce 2 million dan. The cotton fields have increased by about 10% compared to last year. "Ningbo": Regarding Yao cotton, the cotton fields in the area have increased this year, and cotton cultivation has improved. In addition, the weather is favorable. It is estimated that 600,000 dan can be harvested. According to the investigation, the actual harvest last year was 400,000 dan.

American Cotton Traders Buying as Prices Decline

Yesterday, the American cotton market opened with quiet and firm conditions due to traders buying October contracts and a lack of sellers. Prices for all months rose by one to four points. The news regarding the new cotton loan was uncertain, so traders waited for Washington's statement. The weather and harvest news were favorable. Spot demand was stagnant, and factory inventories were low. In the afternoon, the stock market and wheat market were strong, and local firms covered short positions. Liverpool's selling absorbed the long liquidation. Finally, short covering emerged, and Washington's buying caused prices to rise again. Spot prices rose by ten points, and futures prices rose by ten to sixteen points. There was little trading in Indian cotton. Retailers and the public made slight purchases. Plain Goel rose by half a rupee, Olm La rose by 0.25 rupees, and White Row Creek rose by 0.5 to 0.75 rupees. Original telegraph recorded to the left (dated 31st).

According to a telegram from Bombay, the opening forecast for White Row Creek cotton for the April/May term on the 1st was 219 rupees, up two rupees from the previous day's close.

Market Conditions for Three Grades of Yarn and Cotton 178

According to a telegram from Osaka, the spot price of 20s Blue Fish is 214 yen, 20s Red God of Wealth is 218 yen, and 16s Bao Ding and Three Horses are 201 yen, all up by two yen.
